### Assistant
> You’ve got **two separate problems** in what you pasted:
> 
> 1) Your “current HTML” file is **accidentally two pages smashed together** (two `<!DOCTYPE html>`, two `<html>`, two `<head>`, two `<body>`, plus a stray `</main>`). That will absolutely cause inconsistent asset paths and layout weirdness.
> 
> 2) Your **new HTML** uses **no local assets** right now (no favicon, no `/static/tts.js`), so there are **no “paths to update”** unless you want parity with the old page.
> 
> Below is a clean, corrected version of your **new HTML** with the **paths updated** to match what your old page expects, plus a couple of must-fix stability tweaks.

> In that snippet, I left `DOCS_DATA` as `/* keep your existing DOCS_DATA exactly as-is */` so you don’t lose your massive data structure. In your real file, you’ll paste your full `DOCS_DATA` array there.

> ## What you should do next (fast + correct)
> 1) **Fix your “current HTML” file**: decide which page it is (Tailwind “Understanding Q” page *or* the simpler “Cody — Start Here” page) and delete the other. Right now it’s invalid HTML.
> 2) Decide whether `/manual/` and `/faq/` are still real routes in this new doc-app.

> If you tell me your repo structure (just the top-level: `public/`, `static/`, `images/`, etc.), I’ll normalize the paths precisely for Vite/Cloudflare (because `/static/tts.js` might need to be `/tts.js` depending on where you actually place it).

### User
> I think that’s the issue it’s supposed to be static and we were working on updating the flow using folder for topics

### Assistant
> Yes. Right now you’ve built a **single-page JS doc app**, but your mental model (and the older site) is **static, folder-based docs**. Those two architectures fight each other.
> 
> If you want this to be truly **static + folder-per-topic**, you should stop injecting giant HTML strings from `DOCS_DATA` and instead load **real files** from `/docs/...` (or `/manual/...`) with fetch. Then your “flow” is literally your folder tree.
> 
> Here’s the clean approach.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## Target architecture (static + folder topics)
> 
> Use this:
> 
> ```
> /index.html                 (Start Here landing)
> /docs/index.html            (the doc shell w/ sidebar)
> /docs/nav.json              (sidebar map)
> /docs/start.html
> /docs/core/traits.html
> /docs/core/solving.html
> /docs/comms/async.html
> /docs/comms/phone.html
> /docs/boundaries/saying-no.html
> /docs/boundaries/redirect.html
> /docs/family/urgent.html
> /static/tts.js
> /images/favicon.png
> ```
> 
> This is Cloudflare Pages friendly and doesn’t require a build system.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## Step 1 — Replace DOCS_DATA with a nav.json + file loader
> 
> ### `docs/nav.json` (example)
> ```json
> [
>   { "id":"start", "title":"Start Here", "icon":"home", "path":"/docs/start.html" },
> 
>   { "id":"core", "title":"Core Operating System", "icon":"zap", "children":[
>     { "id":"traits", "title":"Core Traits", "path":"/docs/core/traits.html" },
>     { "id":"solving", "title":"Two-Tier Solving", "path":"/docs/core/solving.html" },
>     { "id":"ripple", "title":"Ripple-Check", "path":"/docs/core/ripple.html" }
>   ]},
> 
>   { "id":"comms", "title":"Communication", "icon":"message-square", "children":[
>     { "id":"async", "title":"Async First", "path":"/docs/comms/async.html" },
>     { "id":"phone", "title":"The Phone Rule", "path":"/docs/comms/phone.html" }
>   ]},
> 
>   { "id":"boundaries", "title":"Boundaries & Shade", "icon":"shield", "children":[
>     { "id":"saying-no", "title":"The Power of No", "path":"/docs/boundaries/saying-no.html" },
>     { "id":"redirect", "title":"Snap & Steer", "path":"/docs/boundaries/redirect.html" }
>   ]},
> 
>   { "id":"family", "title":"Family FAQ", "icon":"heart", "children":[
>     { "id":"urgent", "title":"Urgent Access", "path":"/docs/family/urgent.html" }
>   ]}
> ]
> ```
> 
> ---
> 
> ## Step 2 — Update your new HTML JS to load nav.json + HTML files
> 
> In your “new html”, delete `DOCS_DATA` entirely and replace with this logic (drop-in):
> 
> ```html
> <script>
>   const navContainer = document.getElementById('nav-container');
>   const mainContent = document.getElementById('main-content');
>   const breadcrumbTitle = document.getElementById('breadcrumb-title');
> 
>   const sidebar = document.getElementById('sidebar');
>   const overlay = document.getElementById('overlay');
>   const menuBtn = document.getElementById('menu-btn');
> 
>   function safeCreateIcons() {
>     if (window.lucide && typeof window.lucide.createIcons === 'function') lucide.createIcons();
>   }
> 
>   function toggleMenu() {
>     const isClosed = sidebar.classList.contains('-translate-x-full');
>     if (isClosed) { sidebar.classList.remove('-translate-x-full'); overlay.classList.remove('hidden'); }
>     else { sidebar.classList.add('-translate-x-full'); overlay.classList.add('hidden'); }
>   }
>   menuBtn.addEventListener('click', toggleMenu);
>   overlay.addEventListener('click', toggleMenu);
> 
>   let NAV = [];
> 
>   async function fetchNav() {
>     const res = await fetch('/docs/nav.json', { cache: 'no-store' });
>     if (!res.ok) throw new Error('Failed to load /docs/nav.json');
>     NAV = await res.json();
>   }
> 
>   function renderNav() {
>     navContainer.innerHTML = '';
> 
>     NAV.forEach(section => {
>       const hasChildren = Array.isArray(section.children) && section.children.length;
> 
>       const wrapper = document.createElement('div');
>       wrapper.className = 'mb-1';
> 
>       const btn = document.createElement('button');
>       btn.className = `
>         flex items-center justify-between w-full p-3 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium transition-all duration-200
>         text-slate-300 hover:bg-slate-800 nav-item-parent
>       `;
>       btn.id = `nav-${section.id}`;
> 
>       const iconHTML = `<i data-lucide="${section.icon || 'file-text'}" class="w-5 h-5 text-slate-500"></i>`;
>       const chevronHTML = hasChildren ? `<i data-lucide="chevron-right" id="chevron-${section.id}" class="w-4 h-4 text-slate-500 chevron"></i>` : '';
> 
>       btn.innerHTML = `
>         <div class="flex items-center gap-3">
>           ${iconHTML}
>           <span>${section.title}</span>
>         </div>
>         ${chevronHTML}
>       `;
> 
>       if (hasChildren) {
>         btn.onclick = () => toggleAccordion(section.id);
>       } else {
>         btn.onclick = () => loadPath(section.path, section.title, section.id, true);
>       }
> 
>       wrapper.appendChild(btn);
> 
>       if (hasChildren) {
>         const subDiv = document.createElement('div');
>         subDiv.id = `sub-${section.id}`;
>         subDiv.className = 'sub-menu ml-4 border-l border-slate-800 space-y-1 mt-1';
> 
>         section.children.forEach(child => {
>           const subBtn = document.createElement('button');
>           subBtn.className = `
>             flex items-center w-full p-2 pl-6 rounded-lg text-sm text-slate-400
>             hover:text-slate-200 hover:bg-slate-800/50 transition-colors nav-item
>           `;
>           subBtn.id = `nav-${child.id}`;
>           subBtn.textContent = child.title;
>           subBtn.onclick = () => loadPath(child.path, child.title, child.id, false);
>           subDiv.appendChild(subBtn);
>         });
> 
>         wrapper.appendChild(subDiv);
>       }
> 
>       navContainer.appendChild(wrapper);
>     });
> 
>     safeCreateIcons();
>   }
> 
>   function toggleAccordion(id) {
>     const subMenu = document.getElementById(`sub-${id}`);
>     const chevron = document.getElementById(`chevron-${id}`);
>     if (!subMenu) return;
> 
>     const open = subMenu.classList.toggle('open');
>     if (chevron) chevron.classList.toggle('rotate', open);
>   }
> 
>   async function loadPath(path, title, id, isParent) {
>     const res = await fetch(path, { cache: 'no-store' });
>     if (!res.ok) {
>       mainContent.innerHTML = `<div class="text-red-300">Missing file: <span class="font-mono">${path}</span></div>`;
>       return;
>     }
> 
>     const html = await res.text();
>     mainContent.innerHTML = html;
>     breadcrumbTitle.textContent = title;
> 
>     document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active'));
>     document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item-parent').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active','border-l-2','border-purple-500','bg-slate-800','text-white','shadow-lg'));
> 
>     const active = document.getElementById(`nav-${id}`);
>     if (active) {
>       if (isParent) active.classList.add('active','border-l-2','border-purple-500','bg-slate-800','text-white','shadow-lg');
>       else active.classList.add('active');
>     }
> 
>     if (window.innerWidth < 1024 && !sidebar.classList.contains('-translate-x-full')) toggleMenu();
> 
>     safeCreateIcons();
>     window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
>     history.replaceState(null, '', `?p=${encodeURIComponent(path)}`);
>   }
> 
>   function getInitialPath() {
>     const p = new URLSearchParams(location.search).get('p');
>     return p ? decodeURIComponent(p) : '/docs/start.html';
>   }
> 
>   (async function init() {
>     await fetchNav();
>     renderNav();
>     await loadPath(getInitialPath(), 'Start Here', 'start', true);
>   })();
> </script>
> ```
> 
> What this gives you:
> - The **sidebar is driven by folders/files**, not embedded strings.
> - Each doc page is a **real file you can edit directly**.
> - URLs persist via `?p=/docs/.../page.html` without needing a router.
> 
> ---
>

> 
>   <div class="space-y-4">
>     <div class="border-l-2 border-emerald-500 pl-4 py-1">
>       <h3 class="text-lg font-bold text-slate-200">Balanced Energy</h3>
>       <p class="text-slate-400 text-sm">I do not sprint. I maintain a steady, sustainable pace to ensure longevity and quality.</p>
>     </div>
>   </div>
> </div>
> ```

> 
> ## Blunt truth: pick one model
> - If you want **folder topics**, go **static file loader** (above).
> - If you want **one HTML file**, keep the `DOCS_DATA` approach—but then stop talking about folders as the source of truth.
> 
> Your current situation is “trying to get the benefits of both,” and that’s why it feels off.
> 
> If you paste your **current folder tree** (just the paths you have in the repo right now), I’ll map it to the exact `nav.json` and the exact file paths you should use (no guessing).

### User
> Ok what I want is a static doc style personal docs site where family can go and learn about me, my history, struggles, dive deep into topics, preview books with link to purchase, and learn about themselves too by using the questionnaires and tools, listen to audios and view my podcast embedded playlist or embed YouTube videos we were going to use a standard template of a article format where the first part is the short FAQ topic then they can click deep dive to go down and listen to the audio video read the report ect and we were going to do a way to track completion progress for a Microsoft kb style learning module.

### Assistant
> Understood. What you want is not “a single page with injected content.” You want a **static knowledge base + learning path layer**.
> 
> The clean way to do this (static, Cloudflare Pages–friendly, no database) is:
> 
> 1) **Folder-based articles** (real HTML files you can edit)
> 2) A **single reusable article template** that supports:
>    - “FAQ first”
>    - “Deep Dive” sections (audio/video/report/tools)
>    - “Buy / preview book” CTAs
> 3) A **client-side progress tracker** (localStorage) that acts like a Microsoft Learn/KBase completion bar
> 4) A **nav + module manifest** in JSON so the site can render:
>    - sidebar / TOC
>    - learning modules
>    - progress %
> 
> No build required. Fully static.
>

> 
> # 1) Information architecture (the thing you’re actually describing)
> 
> ### Top-level sections
> - **Start Here**
> - **Family FAQs** (quick answers, low friction)
> - **The Manual** (deep dive)
> - **History / Timeline** (your arc)
> - **Struggles / Context** (foreclosure, stability, etc.)
> - **Books** (previews + purchase links)
> - **Tools & Questionnaires** (self-assessments)
> - **Audio / Podcast / YouTube** (embedded playlists)
> - **Learning Paths** (module sets that track completion)
> 
> That maps cleanly to folders.

> # 3) The standard “article template” you described
> 
> Every article should follow the same internal structure so the UI can do nice things (deep dive toggles, progress, etc.).
> 
> Here’s the exact template (drop into every article file under `/docs/articles/...`):
> 
> ```html
> <article class="kb-article space-y-8" data-article-id="manual_core_traits" data-module-tags="manual,core">
>   <!-- Title block -->
>   <header class="space-y-2">
>     <div class="text-xs font-mono tracking-widest uppercase text-emerald-400">FAQ + Deep Dive</div>
>     <h1 class="text-3xl md:text-4xl font-bold text-slate-100">Core Traits</h1>
>     <p class="text-slate-400 max-w-2xl">
>       The quick version of how I operate, plus the deeper context if you want it.
>     </p>
> 
>     <!-- Progress UI hook -->
>     <div class="mt-4 flex items-center gap-3">
>       <button class="kb-complete btn btn-primary" data-complete>
>         Mark as complete
>       </button>
>       <span class="text-xs text-slate-500">Saved on this device</span>
>     </div>
>   </header>
> 
>   <!-- FAQ (short, skimmable) -->
>   <section class="kb-faq space-y-4">
>     <h2 class="text-xl font-semibold text-slate-200">Quick FAQ</h2>
> 
>     <div class="rounded-xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-900/40 p-5">
>       <h3 class="font-semibold text-slate-200">What should you assume by default?</h3>
>       <p class="text-slate-400 mt-1">
>         I’m optimizing for sustainability and clarity. Direct doesn’t mean hostile.
>       </p>
>     </div>
> 
>     <div class="rounded-xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-900/40 p-5">
>       <h3 class="font-semibold text-slate-200">What helps most?</h3>
>       <p class="text-slate-400 mt-1">
>         Text first. Give context + what you need + a time window.
>       </p>
>     </div>
>   </section>
> 
>   <!-- Deep Dive Jump -->
>   <section class="kb-deepdive">
>     <button class="btn btn-ghost" data-jump="#deep-dive">
>       Deep Dive ↓ (audio, video, receipts)
>     </button>
>   </section>
> 
>   <!-- Deep Dive (rich content) -->
>   <section id="deep-dive" class="space-y-6 pt-6 border-t border-white/10">
>     <h2 class="text-2xl font-semibold text-slate-100">Deep Dive</h2>
> 
>     <!-- Audio -->
>     <div class="rounded-xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-900/30 p-5 space-y-3">
>       <h3 class="font-semibold text-slate-200">Listen</h3>
>       <audio controls class="w-full">
>         <source src="/media/audio/core-traits.mp3" type="audio/mpeg">
>       </audio>
>       <p class="text-xs text-slate-500">If audio fails, download: <a class="underline" href="/media/audio/core-traits.mp3">core-traits.mp3</a></p>
>     </div>
> 
>     <!-- YouTube -->
>     <div class="rounded-xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-900/30 p-5 space-y-3">
>       <h3 class="font-semibold text-slate-200">Watch</h3>
>       <div class="aspect-video w-full overflow-hidden rounded-lg border border-white/10">
>         <iframe class="w-full h-full"
>           src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/VIDEO_ID"
>           title="YouTube video"
>           frameborder="0"
>           allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture"
>           allowfullscreen></iframe>
>       </div>
>     </div>
> 
>     <!-- Report / receipts -->
>     <div class="rounded-xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-900/30 p-5 space-y-2">
>       <h3 class="font-semibold text-slate-200">Receipts / Reference</h3>
>       <ul class="list-disc list-inside text-slate-400">
>         <li><a class="underline" href="/docs/assets/core_traits_reference.pdf">Core Traits (PDF)</a></li>
>         <li><a class="underline" href="/docs/assets/core_traits_notes.html">Expanded Notes</a></li>
>       </ul>
>     </div>
> 
>     <!-- Tool -->
>     <div class="rounded-xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-900/30 p-5 space-y-2">
>       <h3 class="font-semibold text-slate-200">Self-check Tool</h3>
>       <p class="text-slate-400">Try the questionnaire linked below.</p>
>       <a class="btn btn-primary" href="/docs/articles/tools/infj_questionnaire.html">Open Questionnaire</a>
>     </div>
>   </section>
> 
>   <!-- CTA -->
>   <section class="pt-6 border-t border-white/10">
>     <div class="rounded-xl border border-purple-500/20 bg-purple-900/10 p-5">
>       <h3 class="font-semibold text-purple-200">Related Book Preview</h3>
>       <p class="text-slate-300 mt-1">If this resonates, you’ll probably want the longer form.</p>
>       <div class="flex flex-wrap gap-3 mt-4">
>         <a class="btn btn-primary" href="/docs/articles/books/713_preview.html">Preview 713</a>
>         <a class="btn btn-ghost" href="https://BUY_LINK" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Purchase</a>
>       </div>
>     </div>
>   </section>
> </article>
> ```
> 
> This gives you: **FAQ first + deep dive + embedded media + tools + book CTA + completion marker**.
> 
> ---
> 
> # 4) “Microsoft KB style learning module” progress (static)
> 
> You can do completion tracking with **localStorage**. That means:
> - No sign-in
> - No backend
> - Works instantly
> - Downside: progress is per-device/browser
> 
> That’s still usually perfect for “family learning resource.”
> 
> ### How it works
> - Each article has `data-article-id="..."`.
> - A JS file records completion state: `kb_complete:<article-id> = true`
> - Module pages compute % complete by reading module lists from `modules.json`
> 
> ---
> 
> # 5) What you need to decide (quick, no rabbit hole)
> 
> There are two “levels” of progress tracking:
> 
> ### Option A (fast, solid): Local progress only
> - localStorage
> - “Mark complete”
> - Module progress bar
> - No accounts
> 
> ### Option B (heavier): Shared progress across devices
> - needs authentication + a store (Cloudflare KV/D1)
> - more engineering, more risk
> 
> Given your goal and time, Option A is the correct first implementation.
> 
> ---
> 
> # 6) The next concrete build steps (the shortest path)
> 
> 1) Create `/docs/index.html` as the “shell” (sidebar + content area) — basically your new HTML, but with the loader approach.
> 2) Create `/docs/nav.json` for navigation.
> 3) Create `/docs/modules.json` defining learning paths.
> 4) Create `/static/progress.js` to:
>    - mark complete
>    - render completion status
>    - compute module completion
> 5) Start converting your content into `/docs/articles/.../*.html` using the standard template.
> 
> ---

> 3) `/static/progress.js` that implements:
>    - mark complete button
>    - “completed” badges in the nav
>    - module progress bar
>

> - `https://qially.me/` (root) or

### Assistant
> Good. Since you’re deploying at the **domain root** (`https://qially.me/`), we’ll build everything with **root-absolute paths** (`/docs/...`, `/static/...`, `/images/...`). That keeps Cloudflare Pages happy and avoids the “subpath breakage” problem.
> 
> Below are the **4 core files** you need to move from “concept” to a working, **mobile-first static KB + learning modules + completion tracking**.

> # 1) `/docs/index.html` (mobile-first doc shell + loader + sidebar + progress)
> 
> Paste this as `docs/index.html`:
> 
> ```html
> <!DOCTYPE html>
> <html lang="en" class="scroll-smooth">
> <head>
>   <meta charset="UTF-8" />
>   <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width,initial-scale=1.0" />
>   <title>Understanding Cody | Personal Docs</title>
> 
>   <link rel="icon" type="image/png" href="/images/favicon.png" />
> 
>   <script src="https://cdn.tailwindcss.com"></script>
>   <script src="https://unpkg.com/lucide@latest"></script>
> 
>   <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:wght@300;400;600;700&family=JetBrains+Mono:wght@400;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
> 
>   <style>
>     body { font-family: Inter, system-ui, -apple-system, Segoe UI, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; }
>     .font-mono { font-family: "JetBrains Mono", ui-monospace, SFMono-Regular, Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, monospace; }
> 
>     ::-webkit-scrollbar { width: 6px; }
>     ::-webkit-scrollbar-track { background: #020617; }
>     ::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb { background: #334155; border-radius: 10px; }
>     ::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb:hover { background: #475569; }
> 
>     .sub-menu { transition: max-height .25s ease, opacity .25s ease; max-height: 0; opacity: 0; overflow: hidden; }
>     .sub-menu.open { max-height: 800px; opacity: 1; }
> 
>     .chevron { transition: transform .2s; }
>     .chevron.rotate { transform: rotate(90deg); } /* right -> down */
> 
>     .nav-leaf.active { background: rgba(16,185,129,.10); color: #34d399; }
>     .nav-parent.active { border-left-color: #a855f7; background: #1e293b; color: #fff; }
> 
>     /* Buttons */
>     .btn { display:inline-flex; align-items:center; justify-content:center; gap:.5rem; padding:.65rem .85rem; border-radius:.75rem; border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.10); background: rgba(255,255,255,.04); font-weight:650; }
>     .btn:hover { transform: translateY(-1px); }
>     .btn-primary { border-color: rgba(45,125,255,.55); background: linear-gradient(180deg, rgba(45,125,255,.26), rgba(45,125,255,.10)); }
>     .btn-ghost { background: transparent; }
>   </style>
> 
>   <script>
>     tailwind.config = { theme: { extend: { colors: { slate: { 950: "#020617" } } } } };
>   </script>
> 
>   <script src="/static/progress.js" defer></script>
> </head>
> 
> <body class="bg-slate-950 text-slate-200 antialiased selection:bg-emerald-500/30 selection:text-emerald-200">
> 
>   <!-- Mobile header (mobile-first) -->
>   <div class="lg:hidden sticky top-0 z-50 bg-slate-950/85 backdrop-blur-md border-b border-white/5 px-4 py-3 flex items-center justify-between">
>     <a href="/docs/" class="flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
>       <div class="w-8 h-8 rounded-lg bg-gradient-to-br from-purple-600 to-blue-600 flex items-center justify-center font-bold text-white shrink-0">C</div>
>       <div class="min-w-0">
>         <div class="font-semibold tracking-tight truncate">Understanding Cody</div>
>         <div class="text-[11px] text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-wider truncate">Personal Docs</div>
>       </div>
>     </a>
>     <button id="menu-btn" class="p-2 text-slate-400 hover:text-white" aria-label="Open menu">
>       <i data-lucide="menu"></i>
>     </button>
>   </div>
> 
>   <div class="flex max-w-7xl mx-auto min-h-[calc(100vh-56px)] lg:min-h-screen">
> 
>     <!-- Sidebar -->
>     <aside id="sidebar"
>       class="fixed inset-y-0 left-0 z-40 w-72 bg-slate-950 border-r border-white/5
>              transform -translate-x-full transition-transform duration-300 ease-in-out
>              lg:translate-x-0 lg:static lg:sticky lg:top-0 lg:h-screen overflow-y-auto">
> 
>       <div class="p-5 lg:p-6">
>         <!-- Desktop brand -->
>         <div class="hidden lg:flex items-center gap-3 mb-6">
>           <div class="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-br from-purple-600 to-blue-600 shadow-lg shadow-purple-900/40 flex items-center justify-center font-bold text-lg text-white">C</div>
>           <div>
>             <h1 class="font-bold text-slate-100 leading-tight">Understanding Cody</h1>
>             <p class="text-xs text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Personal Docs</p>
>           </div>
>         </div>
> 
>         <!-- Overall progress -->
>         <div class="mb-5 p-3 rounded-xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-900/20">
>           <div class="flex items-center justify-between text-xs text-slate-400 mb-2">
>             <span class="font-mono uppercase tracking-wider">Progress</span>
>             <span id="overall-pct" class="font-mono">0%</span>
>           </div>
>           <div class="h-2 rounded-full bg-white/5 overflow-hidden">
>             <div id="overall-bar" class="h-full w-0 bg-emerald-500"></div>
>           </div>
>           <div class="mt-2 text-[11px] text-slate-500">
>             Saved locally on this device.
>           </div>
>         </div>
> 
>         <nav id="nav-container" class="space-y-1"></nav>
>       </div>
> 
>       <div class="mt-auto p-5 lg:p-6 bg-gradient-to-t from-slate-950 to-transparent border-t border-white/5">
>         <p class="text-xs text-slate-600 text-center">
>           &copy; <span id="year"></span> Cody<br/>
>           Updated: Dec 2025
>         </p>
>       </div>
>     </aside>
> 
>     <!-- Mobile overlay -->
>     <div id="overlay" class="fixed inset-0 bg-black/60 z-30 hidden lg:hidden backdrop-blur-sm"></div>
> 
>     <!-- Main content -->
>     <main class="flex-1 p-4 sm:p-6 lg:p-10 max-w-4xl mx-auto w-full">
>       <div class="hidden md:flex items-center gap-2 text-xs font-mono text-slate-500 mb-6 uppercase tracking-wider">
>         <i data-lucide="home" class="w-3 h-3"></i>
>         <span>/</span><span>Docs</span><span>/</span>
>         <span id="breadcrumb-title" class="text-purple-400">Start Here</span>
>       </div>
> 
>       <!-- Module header (optional; filled when on module pages) -->
>       <section id="module-header" class="hidden mb-6 p-4 rounded-xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-900/20">
>         <div class="flex items-start justify-between gap-4">
>           <div>
>             <div class="text-xs text-slate-500 font-mono uppercase tracking-wider">Learning Path</div>
>             <h2 id="module-title" class="text-lg font-semibold text-slate-100">Module</h2>
>             <p id="module-desc" class="text-sm text-slate-400 mt-1"></p>
>           </div>
>           <div class="text-right shrink-0">
>             <div class="text-xs text-slate-500 font-mono uppercase tracking-wider">Completion</div>
>             <div id="module-pct" class="text-xl font-bold text-emerald-400">0%</div>
>           </div>
>         </div>
>         <div class="mt-3 h-2 rounded-full bg-white/5 overflow-hidden">
>           <div id="module-bar" class="h-full w-0 bg-emerald-500"></div>
>         </div>
>       </section>
> 
>       <div id="main-content" class="min-h-[60vh]"></div>
> 
>       <div class="mt-14 pt-6 border-t border-white/5 flex flex-col sm:flex-row justify-between items-start sm:items-center gap-4 text-sm text-slate-500">
>         <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
>           <div class="w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-emerald-500 animate-pulse"></div>
>           System Status: Operational
>         </div>
>         <div class="flex gap-4">
>           <a class="hover:text-purple-300 transition-colors" href="/docs/?p=/docs/articles/faq/how_to_help.html">How to help</a>
>           <a class="hover:text-purple-300 transition-colors" href="/">Home</a>
>         </div>
>       </div>
>     </main>
>   </div>
> 
>   <script>
>     const navContainer = document.getElementById("nav-container");
>     const mainContent = document.getElementById("main-content");
>     const breadcrumbTitle = document.getElementById("breadcrumb-title");
>     const yearSpan = document.getElementById("year");
> 
>     const sidebar = document.getElementById("sidebar");
>     const overlay = document.getElementById("overlay");
>     const menuBtn = document.getElementById("menu-btn");
> 
>     const moduleHeader = document.getElementById("module-header");
>     const moduleTitle = document.getElementById("module-title");
>     const moduleDesc = document.getElementById("module-desc");
>     const modulePct = document.getElementById("module-pct");
>     const moduleBar = document.getElementById("module-bar");
> 
>     yearSpan.textContent = new Date().getFullYear();
> 
>     function safeIcons() {
>       if (window.lucide && typeof window.lucide.createIcons === "function") lucide.createIcons();
>     }
> 
>     function toggleMenu() {
>       const closed = sidebar.classList.contains("-translate-x-full");
>       if (closed) { sidebar.classList.remove("-translate-x-full"); overlay.classList.remove("hidden"); }
>       else { sidebar.classList.add("-translate-x-full"); overlay.classList.add("hidden"); }
>     }
>     menuBtn.addEventListener("click", toggleMenu);
>     overlay.addEventListener("click", toggleMenu);
> 
>     let NAV = [];
>     let MODULES = [];
> 
>     async function fetchJson(path) {
>       const res = await fetch(path, { cache: "no-store" });
>       if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to load ${path}`);
>       return await res.json();
>     }
> 
>     function setActiveNav(id, isParent) {
>       document.querySelectorAll(".nav-leaf").forEach(el => el.classList.remove("active"));
>       document.querySelectorAll(".nav-parent").forEach(el => el.classList.remove("active","border-l-2","border-purple-500","bg-slate-800","text-white","shadow-lg"));
> 
>       const active = document.getElementById(`nav-${id}`);
>       if (!active) return;
> 
>       if (isParent) active.classList.add("active","border-l-2","border-purple-500","bg-slate-800","text-white","shadow-lg");
>       else active.classList.add("active");
>     }
> 
>     function toggleAccordion(id) {
>       const sub = document.getElementById(`sub-${id}`);
>       const chev = document.getElementById(`chev-${id}`);
>       if (!sub) return;
> 
>       const open = sub.classList.toggle("open");
>       if (chev) chev.classList.toggle("rotate", open);
>     }
> 
>     function renderNav() {
>       navContainer.innerHTML = "";
> 
>       NAV.forEach(section => {
>         const hasChildren = Array.isArray(section.children) && section.children.length;
> 
>         const wrapper = document.createElement("div");
>         wrapper.className = "mb-1";
> 
>         const btn = document.createElement("button");
>         btn.id = `nav-${section.id}`;
>         btn.className = `
>           nav-parent flex items-center justify-between w-full p-3 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium
>           transition-colors text-slate-300 hover:bg-slate-800
>         `;
> 
>         btn.innerHTML = `
>           <div class="flex items-center gap-3 min-w-0">
>             <i data-lucide="${section.icon || "file-text"}" class="w-5 h-5 text-slate-500 shrink-0"></i>
>             <span class="truncate">${section.title}</span>
>           </div>
>           ${hasChildren ? `<i data-lucide="chevron-right" id="chev-${section.id}" class="w-4 h-4 text-slate-500 chevron"></i>` : ``}
>         `;
> 
>         if (hasChildren) btn.onclick = () => toggleAccordion(section.id);
>         else btn.onclick = () => loadPath(section.path, section.title, section.id, true);
> 
>         wrapper.appendChild(btn);
> 
>         if (hasChildren) {
>           const subDiv = document.createElement("div");
>           subDiv.id = `sub-${section.id}`;
>           subDiv.className = "sub-menu ml-4 border-l border-slate-800 space-y-1 mt-1";
> 
>           section.children.forEach(child => {
>             const subBtn = document.createElement("button");
>             subBtn.id = `nav-${child.id}`;
>             subBtn.className = `
>               nav-leaf flex items-center justify-between w-full p-2 pl-6 rounded-lg text-sm
>               text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-200 hover:bg-slate-800/50 transition-colors
>             `;
> 
>             subBtn.innerHTML = `
>               <span class="truncate">${child.title}</span>
>               <span class="ml-2 text-[10px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full border border-white/10 text-slate-500"
>                     data-complete-badge="${child.articleId || ""}"> </span>
>             `;
> 
>             subBtn.onclick = () => loadPath(child.path, child.title, child.id, false, child.articleId);
>             subDiv.appendChild(subBtn);
>           });
> 
>           wrapper.appendChild(subDiv);
>         }
> 
>         navContainer.appendChild(wrapper);
>       });
> 
>       safeIcons();
>     }
> 
>     function showModuleHeaderIfApplicable(path) {
>       // Module pages are plain articles too, but we can show a header if path matches a module entry.
>       const mod = MODULES.find(m => m.landing && m.landing === path);
>       if (!mod) {
>         moduleHeader.classList.add("hidden");
>         return;
>       }
> 
>       moduleTitle.textContent = mod.title;
>       moduleDesc.textContent = mod.description || "";
>       moduleHeader.classList.remove("hidden");
> 
>       const pct = window.KBProgress?.modulePercent(mod) ?? 0;
>       modulePct.textContent = `${pct}%`;
>       moduleBar.style.width = `${pct}%`;
>     }
> 
>     async function loadPath(path, title, navId, isParent, explicitArticleId) {
>       const res = await fetch(path, { cache: "no-store" });
>       if (!res.ok) {
>         mainContent.innerHTML = `<div class="p-4 rounded-xl border border-red-500/20 bg-red-900/10 text-red-200">
>           Missing file: <span class="font-mono">${path}</span>
>         </div>`;
>         return;
>       }
> 
>       const html = await res.text();
>       mainContent.innerHTML = html;
>       breadcrumbTitle.textContent = title;
> 
>       setActiveNav(navId, isParent);
> 
>       // Initialize completion + deep-dive jumps inside loaded content
>       if (window.KBProgress) {
>         window.KBProgress.initArticle(mainContent, explicitArticleId);
>         window.KBProgress.refreshBadges();
>         window.KBProgress.refreshOverall();
>       }
> 
>       showModuleHeaderIfApplicable(path);
> 
>       if (window.innerWidth < 1024 && !sidebar.classList.contains("-translate-x-full")) toggleMenu();
>       safeIcons();
>       window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: "smooth" });
>       history.replaceState(null, "", `/docs/?p=${encodeURIComponent(path)}`);
>     }
> 
>     function getInitialPath() {
>       const p = new URLSearchParams(location.search).get("p");
>       return p ? decodeURIComponent(p) : "/docs/articles/start.html";
>     }
> 
>     (async function init() {
>       NAV = await fetchJson("/docs/nav.json");
>       MODULES = await fetchJson("/docs/modules.json");
> 
>       renderNav();
> 
>       // Defer progress init until modules load
>       if (window.KBProgress) {
>         window.KBProgress.setModules(MODULES);
>       }
> 
>       await loadPath(getInitialPath(), "Start Here", "start", true, "start_here");
>     })();
>   </script>
> </body>
> </html>
> ```
> 
> ---

> # 4) `/static/progress.js` (completion tracking, badges, overall %, deep-dive jump)
> 
> Paste as `static/progress.js`:
> 
> ```js
> (function () {
>   const KEY_PREFIX = "kb_complete:";
>   let MODULES = [];
> 
>   function isComplete(articleId) {
>     return localStorage.getItem(KEY_PREFIX + articleId) === "1";
>   }
> 
>   function setComplete(articleId, value) {
>     if (!articleId) return;
>     localStorage.setItem(KEY_PREFIX + articleId, value ? "1" : "0");
>   }
> 
>   function articleIdFromDOM(container, explicitArticleId) {
>     if (explicitArticleId) return explicitArticleId;
>     const el = container.querySelector("[data-article-id]");
>     return el ? el.getAttribute("data-article-id") : null;
>   }
> 
>   function bindDeepDiveJumps(container) {
>     container.querySelectorAll("[data-jump]").forEach(btn => {
>       btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
>         const target = btn.getAttribute("data-jump");
>         const node = container.querySelector(target);
>         if (node) node.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth", block: "start" });
>       });
>     });
>   }
> 
>   function initCompleteButton(container, explicitArticleId) {
>     const id = articleIdFromDOM(container, explicitArticleId);
>     if (!id) return;
> 
>     const btn = container.querySelector("[data-complete]");
>     if (!btn) return;
> 
>     const applyState = () => {
>       const done = isComplete(id);
>       btn.textContent = done ? "Completed ✓" : "Mark as complete";
>       btn.classList.toggle("btn-primary", !done);
>       btn.classList.toggle("btn-ghost", done);
>     };
> 
>     btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
>       const next = !isComplete(id);
>       setComplete(id, next);
>       applyState();
>       refreshBadges();
>       refreshOverall();
>     });
> 
>     applyState();
>   }
> 
>   function refreshBadges() {
>     document.querySelectorAll("[data-complete-badge]").forEach(el => {
>       const id = el.getAttribute("data-complete-badge");
>       if (!id) return;
>       el.textContent = isComplete(id) ? "✓" : "";
>       el.classList.toggle("text-emerald-400", isComplete(id));
>     });
>   }
> 
>   function allArticleIds() {
>     // Union from modules + any explicit “known” ids
>     const ids = new Set();
>     MODULES.forEach(m => m.items.forEach(it => ids.add(it.articleId)));
>     return Array.from(ids);
>   }
> 
>   function overallPercent() {
>     const ids = allArticleIds();
>     if (!ids.length) return 0;
>     const done = ids.filter(isComplete).length;
>     return Math.round((done / ids.length) * 100);
>   }
> 
>   function refreshOverall() {
>     const pct = overallPercent();
>     const pctEl = document.getElementById("overall-pct");
>     const barEl = document.getElementById("overall-bar");
>     if (pctEl) pctEl.textContent = pct + "%";
>     if (barEl) barEl.style.width = pct + "%";
>   }
> 
>   function modulePercent(moduleObj) {
>     if (!moduleObj || !moduleObj.items || !moduleObj.items.length) return 0;
>     const done = moduleObj.items.filter(it => isComplete(it.articleId)).length;
>     return Math.round((done / moduleObj.items.length) * 100);
>   }
> 
>   function setModules(mods) {
>     MODULES = Array.isArray(mods) ? mods : [];
>     refreshBadges();
>     refreshOverall();
>   }
> 
>   function initArticle(container, explicitArticleId) {
>     bindDeepDiveJumps(container);
>     initCompleteButton(container, explicitArticleId);
>   }
> 
>   window.KBProgress = {
>     setModules,
>     initArticle,
>     refreshBadges,
>     refreshOverall,
>     modulePercent
>   };
> })();
> ```
> 
> ---
> 
> # 5) Minimal starter articles (so it actually runs)
> 
> Create these files (copy/paste stubs). They’re mobile-first by default because the shell is.
> 
> ### `/docs/articles/start.html`
> ```html
> <article class="space-y-8" data-article-id="start_here">
>   <header class="space-y-3">
>     <div class="text-xs font-mono tracking-widest uppercase text-emerald-400">Private Resource</div>
>     <h1 class="text-3xl sm:text-4xl font-bold text-slate-100">Start Here</h1>
>     <p class="text-slate-400 max-w-2xl">
>       This site explains how I operate, what’s been happening, and how to support me without confusion.
>       Start with the FAQs if you want the short version.
>     </p>
> 
>     <div class="flex flex-wrap gap-3 pt-2">
>       <a class="btn btn-primary" href="/docs/?p=/docs/articles/faq/why_no_phone.html">FAQs</a>
>       <a class="btn" href="/docs/?p=/docs/articles/modules/family_start.html">Learning Path</a>
>     </div>
>   </header>
> 
>   <section class="space-y-4">
>     <h2 class="text-xl font-semibold text-slate-200">Quick Status</h2>
>     <div class="rounded-xl border border-purple-500/20 bg-purple-900/10 p-5">
>       <p class="text-slate-300">
>         Default is asynchronous communication. If it’s truly urgent: text with purpose + a time window.
>       </p>
>     </div>
>   </section>
> 
>   <div class="pt-4">
>     <button class="btn btn-primary" data-complete>Mark as complete</button>
>     <span class="ml-2 text-xs text-slate-500">Saved on this device</span>
>   </div>
> </article>
> ```
> 
> ### `/docs/articles/modules/family_start.html`
> ```html
> <article class="space-y-6" data-article-id="lp_family">
>   <header>
>     <div class="text-xs font-mono tracking-widest uppercase text-emerald-400">Learning Path</div>
>     <h1 class="text-3xl font-bold text-slate-100">Family: Start Here</h1>
>     <p class="text-slate-400 mt-2">Complete these pages to get the “functional understanding” without overwhelm.</p>
>   </header>
> 
>   <div class="rounded-xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-900/20 p-5 space-y-3">
>     <h2 class="text-lg font-semibold text-slate-200">Checklist</h2>
>     <ul class="list-disc list-inside text-slate-400 space-y-1">
>       <li><a class="underline" href="/docs/?p=/docs/articles/start.html">Start Here</a></li>
>       <li><a class="underline" href="/docs/?p=/docs/articles/faq/why_no_phone.html">Why I don’t answer the phone</a></li>
>       <li><a class="underline" href="/docs/?p=/docs/articles/faq/how_to_help.html">How to help</a></li>
>     </ul>
>   </div>
> 
>   <div class="pt-2">
>     <button class="btn btn-primary" data-complete>Mark module page complete</button>
>   </div>
> </article>
> ```
> 
> (Repeat this pattern for your other articles.)
> 
> ---
> 
> ## Straight talk: this gets you 80% of what you described
> - Static docs site
> - Mobile-first UI
> - FAQ-first + deep dive structure (per article)
> - Embeds (YouTube/audio) work in pure HTML
> - Completion tracking + progress bar (local)
> - “Microsoft Learn style” learning paths via `modules.json`
> 
> The remaining 20% (shared progress across devices, logins, personalized quizzes, analytics) can come later **without rewriting the content**.
> 
> If you want, tell me which two pages you want written first:
> 1) **Why I don’t answer the phone** (FAQ + deep dive + audio/video placeholders)
> 2) **How to help (without chaos)** (clear instructions + donation/help CTAs + boundaries)
> 
> …and I’ll generate them in the exact article template so you can drop them into `/docs/articles/faq/`.

### User
> What about the main landing page?

### Assistant
> You need a **separate, simpler landing page** at `/index.html` that funnels people into the docs experience without dumping them into a sidebar immediately—especially on mobile.
> 
> Best practice for your use case:
> 
> - `/index.html` = “front door” with 3–5 clear choices (FAQs, Start Here, Learning Path, Books, Media)
> - `/docs/` = the KB shell (sidebar + progress + articles)
> 
> Here’s a **mobile-first** `/index.html` that matches your aesthetic and routes cleanly into your docs paths on `qially.me`.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## `/index.html` (mobile-first landing page)
> 
> ```html
> <!doctype html>
> <html lang="en">

> 
> ### Why this is the right landing page
> - **Mobile-first**: one column, large tap targets, simple choices.
> - **Doesn’t depend on the docs shell** to “explain itself.”
> - Links go directly to the most useful “first clicks.”
> - Keeps your “private resource” vibe without adding auth complexity.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## Where it lives / routing
> - This file is your root: `https://qially.me/`
> - Docs shell: `https://qially.me/docs/` (served by `docs/index.html`)
> - Articles load via: `https://qially.me/docs/?p=/docs/articles/...`
> 
> ---
> 
> ## One more blunt correction
> If you want `/docs/` to load when someone clicks “Docs”, make sure Cloudflare Pages is set up so that `/docs/` serves `/docs/index.html`. With static hosting, that happens automatically if the folder contains an `index.html` (which we did).
> 
> ---
> 
> If you want, I can also produce a **locked-down “private” landing variant** that adds a simple passcode gate (still static) using localStorage. It won’t be real security like Zero Trust, but it stops random drive-bys.

### User
> I love the look and feel of this so much I can’t wait to start to build it out with content this feels like the most coherent site docs yet for my wiki to my family

### Assistant
> Good — that reaction tells me we finally matched **what you’ve been holding in your head**.
> 
> Let me ground this so you don’t lose momentum or accidentally over-engineer it.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## Why this finally feels *right* (and not just “pretty”)
> 
> This setup works because it aligns **structure, psychology, and reality**:
> 
> ### 1. Cognitive load is correct (especially for family)
> - Landing page = **choice, not explanation**
> - Docs = **progressive disclosure**
> - Articles = **FAQ → Deep Dive**
> That mirrors how *humans* actually learn under emotional stress.
> 
> ### 2. It respects boundaries *by design*
> You’re no longer explaining yourself repeatedly.
> The site:
> - answers the same questions once
> - sets communication rules passively
> - lets people self-educate without pulling you into chaos
> 
> That’s not aesthetic — that’s operational self-defense.
> 
> ### 3. It’s modular and honest
> You can:
> - add content when you have energy
> - leave sections unfinished without “breaking” anything
> - expand books, tools, or history **without refactoring**
> 
> That’s why it feels coherent. Nothing is fighting the grain.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## How to build this out *without overwhelming yourself*
> 
> Here’s the **only build order I recommend**. Anything else is a trap.
> 
> ### Phase 1 — Anchor pages (do these first)
> These reduce incoming noise the fastest.
> 
> 1. `/docs/articles/start.html` ✅ (already done)
> 2. `/docs/articles/faq/why_no_phone.html`
> 3. `/docs/articles/faq/how_to_help.html`
> 
> These three alone will change how people interact with you.
> 
> > Rule: Don’t write *everything*. Write **enough that future-you doesn’t have to explain it again**.
> 
> ---
> 
> ### Phase 2 — One learning path only
> Do **Family: Start Here** first.
> 
> - Flesh out `family_start.html`
> - Make sure its checklist matches real behavior you want
> - Ignore the Manual for now
> 
> You’ll feel tempted to jump to “core traits” and “deep theory.”  
> Resist. That’s for later, when the pressure drops.
> 
> ---
> 
> ### Phase 3 — One “Deep Dive” article
> Pick **one** article where:
> - FAQ = calm, plain
> - Deep dive = receipts, audio, context
> 
> This proves the template end-to-end:
> - text
> - audio
> - video
> - completion tracking
> 
> Once one works, the rest are copy-paste and edit.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## Very important constraint (I’m stopping you early on purpose)
> 
> **Do NOT:**
> - add auth yet
> - add analytics yet
> - add comments
> - add forms everywhere
> - add more than one questionnaire tool initially
> 
> All of those increase cognitive and emotional overhead.
> 
> This site is not about “engagement.”
> It’s about **clarity + relief**.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## How to write content that fits this system (quick rule)
> 
> When you write an article, ask:
> 
> > “If I were emotionally flooded, could I skim this and still get the point?”
> 
> If yes → it belongs.
> If it requires patience → push it into the Deep Dive.
> 
> That’s the whole philosophy.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## You’re allowed to feel proud here
> You’ve been trying to:
> - explain yourself
> - document reality
> - protect your energy
> - help people understand you
> 
> …all at once, without a container.
> 
> This site **is the container**.
> 
> When you’re ready, next I can:
> - write the **first FAQ article with you**
> - turn one of your existing explanations into a clean article
> - or help you design the **Needs Check-In tool** to plug into this system
> 
> Just tell me **which page you want to write first** and whether you want:
> - help structuring it
> - or a first draft you can edit
> 
> We’ll build this slowly and correctly — not rushed, not chaotic.

>     <!-- Screen: Completion -->
>     <section id="screen-complete" class="screen">
>         <h2>You've Reached the End of This Loop</h2>
>         <p class="lead">
>             Thanks for taking the time to understand me. You can revisit any chapter or explore the extras below.
>         </p>
>         <div class="choices">
>             <button class="primary" data-go="screen-hub">Revisit any chapter</button>
>             <button class="primary" data-go="screen-extras">Explore Extras & Deep Dives</button>
>         </div>
>     </section>
> 
>     <script>
>         const CHAPTERS = [
>             { id: 'learn', title: 'Learn / How My World Works', screen: 'screen-learn' },
>             { id: 'health', title: 'Health / Brain & Body', screen: 'screen-health' },
>             { id: 'relationships', title: 'Relationships / Boundaries', screen: 'screen-relationships' }
>         ];
> 
>         const STORAGE_KEY = 'manual_to_me_progress_v1';
> 
>         function getVisited() {
>             try {
>                 return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY)) || [];
>             } catch {
>                 return [];
>             }
>         }
> 
>         function setVisited(visited) {
>             localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(visited));
>         }
> 
>         function markVisited(chapterId) {
>             const visited = getVisited();
>             if (!visited.includes(chapterId)) {
>                 visited.push(chapterId);
>                 setVisited(visited);
>             }
>             updateProgressUI();
>         }
> 
>         function showScreen(id) {
>             document.querySelectorAll('.screen').forEach(s => s.classList.remove('active'));
>             const targetScreen = document.getElementById(id);
>             if (targetScreen) {
>                 targetScreen.classList.add('active');
>                 window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
>             }
> 
>             // If this is a chapter screen, mark it visited
>             const chapter = CHAPTERS.find(c => c.screen === id);
>             if (chapter) {
>                 markVisited(chapter.id);
>             }
>         }
> 
>         function updateProgressUI() {
>             const visited = getVisited();
>             const progressText = document.getElementById('progress-text');
>             const progressBar = document.getElementById('progress-bar');
>             const completedList = document.getElementById('completed-list');
>             const choiceButtons = document.getElementById('choice-buttons');
> 
>             const total = CHAPTERS.length;
>             const done = visited.length;
>             const percent = Math.round((done / total) * 100);
> 
>             if (progressText) {
>                 progressText.textContent = `${done}/${total} chapters visited (${percent}%)`;
>             }
>             if (progressBar) {
>                 progressBar.style.width = percent + '%';
>             }
> 
>             // Remaining vs completed chapters
>             const remaining = CHAPTERS.filter(c => !visited.includes(c.id));
>             const completed = CHAPTERS.filter(c => visited.includes(c.id));
> 
>             // Hub choice buttons: only remaining chapters
>             if (choiceButtons) {
>                 choiceButtons.innerHTML = '';
>                 if (remaining.length === 0) {
>                     // All chapters visited, show completion button
>                     const doneBtn = document.createElement('button');
>                     doneBtn.className = 'primary';
>                     doneBtn.textContent = 'Finish this loop';
>                     doneBtn.onclick = () => showScreen('screen-complete');
>                     choiceButtons.appendChild(doneBtn);
>                 } else {
>                     remaining.forEach(ch => {
>                         const btn = document.createElement('button');
>                         btn.className = 'primary';
>                         btn.textContent = ch.title;
>                         btn.onclick = () => showScreen(ch.screen);
>                         choiceButtons.appendChild(btn);
>                     });
>                 }
>             }
> 
>             // Completed section list
>             if (completedList) {
>                 completedList.innerHTML = '';
>                 if (completed.length > 0) {
>                     const header = document.createElement('p');
>                     header.textContent = 'Revisit a completed chapter:';
>                     completedList.appendChild(header);
> 
>                     completed.forEach(ch => {
>                         const btn = document.createElement('button');
>                         btn.textContent = ch.title;
>                         btn.onclick = () => showScreen(ch.screen);
>                         completedList.appendChild(btn);
>                     });
>                 }
>             }
>         }
> 
>         // Wire generic button navigation
>         document.querySelectorAll('button[data-go]').forEach(btn => {
>             btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
>                 showScreen(btn.getAttribute('data-go'));
>             });
>         });
> 
>         // Initialize on load
>         updateProgressUI();
>     </script>
> </body>
> </html>

### Assistant
> You can absolutely use this—just not as a replacement for the KB shell. Think of it as a **guided “Onboarding Tour”** that funnels people into the static docs.
> 
> ### The correct architecture (so you don’t break the coherence you just achieved)
> 
> - `/index.html` = front door (already great)
> - `/docs/` = docs shell (sidebar + progress + articles)
> - **Add**: `/manual/` = **guided “Manual to Me” experience** (your multi-screen flow)
> - The guided flow should **link into** real doc articles for the deep dive and the receipts.
> 
> That gives you the best of both worlds:
> - A *warm, story-driven* entry
> - A *stable, scalable* docs system underneath
> 
> If you try to “merge” the guided flow into the Start Here article, you’ll turn your clean doc architecture into a spaghetti SPA again.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## How to adapt your HTML to fit your new system
> 
> ### Option A (recommended): Make this the manual landing at `/manual/index.html`
> Then each “chapter” button sends them to the corresponding docs pages.
> 
> **Minimal changes:**
> 1) Keep your screens/animations.
> 2) Replace each chapter’s placeholder content with short intro + a “Continue to Deep Dive” link that opens the KB article in `/docs/?p=...`.
> 3) Keep your localStorage progress (it’s fine), but align it with the same `articleId`s used in the docs system.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## Concrete edits to do (surgical)
> 
> ### 1) Put it at `/manual/index.html`
> Also update branding to match your dark/glass vibe if you want consistency (optional).
> 
> ### 2) Replace “chapter screens” with “chapter overview + jump to docs”
> In each chapter screen, keep:
> - the 2-min video embed
> - 3–6 paragraphs max
> - a button row:
> 
> - **Read the FAQ + Deep Dive**
> - **Mark chapter complete**
> - **Back to hub**
> 
> Example replacement inside `#screen-learn`:
> 
> ```html
> <div class="choices">
>   <button class="primary" onclick="goDocs('/docs/articles/manual/core_traits.html')">Open Manual Article</button>
>   <button onclick="goDocs('/docs/articles/history/overview.html')">Read History Overview</button>
>   <button data-go="screen-hub">Back to Choices</button>
> </div>
> ```
> 
> Then add this helper:
> 
> ```html
> <script>
>   function goDocs(path){
>     window.location.href = `/docs/?p=${encodeURIComponent(path)}`;
>   }
> </script>
> ```
> 
> Now your guided manual becomes a **curated portal** into the static wiki.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 3) Align progress keys with your KB progress system
> 
> Right now you store visited chapters under:
> `manual_to_me_progress_v1`
> 
> Your docs system uses:
> `kb_complete:<articleId>`
> 
> Do this instead:
> - When they “visit” a chapter in the manual flow, mark the corresponding KB article complete too (or at least “started”).
> 
> Add this function:
> 
> ```html
> <script>
>   function kbSetComplete(articleId, value=true){
>     try { localStorage.setItem(`kb_complete:${articleId}`, value ? "1" : "0"); } catch {}
>   }
> </script>
> ```
> 
> Then inside `markVisited(chapterId)` map chapters to article IDs:
> 
> ```js
> const CHAPTER_TO_ARTICLE = {
>   learn: "m_core_traits",
>   health: "m_health_overview",
>   relationships: "m_relationships_boundaries"
> };
> 
> function markVisited(chapterId) {
>   const visited = getVisited();
>   if (!visited.includes(chapterId)) {
>     visited.push(chapterId);
>     setVisited(visited);
>   }
> 
>   const articleId = CHAPTER_TO_ARTICLE[chapterId];
>   if (articleId) kbSetComplete(articleId, true);
> 
>   updateProgressUI();
> }
> ```
> 
> Now your manual flow and your docs progress bar speak the same language.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 4) Convert “Extras” playlists into real docs pages too
> Instead of embedding everything only inside the guided flow, make each playlist a docs page:
> 
> - `/docs/articles/media/podcast.html`
> - `/docs/articles/media/youtube.html`
> - `/docs/articles/media/playlists_health.html` etc.
> 
> Then the manual “Extras” screen links out to those pages for evergreen organization.
> 
> ---
> 
> # If you really want it “merged” with Start Here
> Do it like this, without breaking the docs model:
> 
> - Keep `/docs/articles/start.html` as the simple Start Here article
> - Add a single CTA block:
> 
> **“Prefer a guided version?” → `/manual/`**
> 
> That’s it. Don’t embed the entire multi-screen app inside the article loader.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## My recommendation (the cleanest outcome)
> - Use your provided HTML as: **`/manual/index.html`**
> - Keep `/docs/` as the scalable wiki
> - Link between them:
>   - landing → manual or docs
>   - manual → specific docs pages for depth and receipts
> 
> That keeps the coherence, and you get the cinematic onboarding experience you want.
> 
> ---
> 
> If you tell me the three “chapters” you want in the manual flow to map to real docs pages (titles + intended file paths), I’ll rewrite your `CHAPTERS` array + button wiring so it’s immediately functional with your `/docs/articles/...` structure.

>     <!-- Screen: Completion -->
>     <section id="screen-complete" class="screen">
>         <h2>You've Reached the End of This Loop</h2>
>         <p class="lead">
>             Thanks for taking the time to understand me. You can revisit any chapter or explore the extras below.
>         </p>
>         <div class="choices">
>             <button class="primary" data-go="screen-hub">Revisit any chapter</button>
>             <button class="primary" data-go="screen-extras">Explore Extras & Deep Dives</button>
>         </div>
>     </section>
> 
>     <script>
>         const CHAPTERS = [
>             { id: 'learn', title: 'Learn / How My World Works', screen: 'screen-learn' },
>             { id: 'health', title: 'Health / Brain & Body', screen: 'screen-health' },
>             { id: 'relationships', title: 'Relationships / Boundaries', screen: 'screen-relationships' }
>         ];
> 
>         const STORAGE_KEY = 'manual_to_me_progress_v1';
> 
>         function getVisited() {
>             try {
>                 return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY)) || [];
>             } catch {
>                 return [];
>             }
>         }
> 
>         function setVisited(visited) {
>             localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(visited));
>         }
> 
>         function markVisited(chapterId) {
>             const visited = getVisited();
>             if (!visited.includes(chapterId)) {
>                 visited.push(chapterId);
>                 setVisited(visited);
>             }
>             updateProgressUI();
>         }
> 
>         function showScreen(id) {
>             document.querySelectorAll('.screen').forEach(s => s.classList.remove('active'));
>             const targetScreen = document.getElementById(id);
>             if (targetScreen) {
>                 targetScreen.classList.add('active');
>                 window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
>             }
> 
>             // If this is a chapter screen, mark it visited
>             const chapter = CHAPTERS.find(c => c.screen === id);
>             if (chapter) {
>                 markVisited(chapter.id);
>             }
>         }
> 
>         function updateProgressUI() {
>             const visited = getVisited();
>             const progressText = document.getElementById('progress-text');
>             const progressBar = document.getElementById('progress-bar');
>             const completedList = document.getElementById('completed-list');
>             const choiceButtons = document.getElementById('choice-buttons');
> 
>             const total = CHAPTERS.length;
>             const done = visited.length;
>             const percent = Math.round((done / total) * 100);
> 
>             if (progressText) {
>                 progressText.textContent = `${done}/${total} chapters visited (${percent}%)`;
>             }
>             if (progressBar) {
>                 progressBar.style.width = percent + '%';
>             }
> 
>             // Remaining vs completed chapters
>             const remaining = CHAPTERS.filter(c => !visited.includes(c.id));
>             const completed = CHAPTERS.filter(c => visited.includes(c.id));
> 
>             // Hub choice buttons: only remaining chapters
>             if (choiceButtons) {
>                 choiceButtons.innerHTML = '';
>                 if (remaining.length === 0) {
>                     // All chapters visited, show completion button
>                     const doneBtn = document.createElement('button');
>                     doneBtn.className = 'primary';
>                     doneBtn.textContent = 'Finish this loop';
>                     doneBtn.onclick = () => showScreen('screen-complete');
>                     choiceButtons.appendChild(doneBtn);
>                 } else {
>                     remaining.forEach(ch => {
>                         const btn = document.createElement('button');
>                         btn.className = 'primary';
>                         btn.textContent = ch.title;
>                         btn.onclick = () => showScreen(ch.screen);
>                         choiceButtons.appendChild(btn);
>                     });
>                 }
>             }
> 
>             // Completed section list
>             if (completedList) {
>                 completedList.innerHTML = '';
>                 if (completed.length > 0) {
>                     const header = document.createElement('p');
>                     header.textContent = 'Revisit a completed chapter:';
>                     completedList.appendChild(header);
> 
>                     completed.forEach(ch => {
>                         const btn = document.createElement('button');
>                         btn.textContent = ch.title;
>                         btn.onclick = () => showScreen(ch.screen);
>                         completedList.appendChild(btn);
>                     });
>                 }
>             }
>         }
> 
>         // Wire generic button navigation
>         document.querySelectorAll('button[data-go]').forEach(btn => {
>             btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
>                 showScreen(btn.getAttribute('data-go'));
>             });
>         });
> 
>         // Initialize on load
>         updateProgressUI();
>     </script>
> </body>
> </html>

>         <article class="relative pl-10 md:pl-12">
>           <div class="bg-slate-900 border border-slate-800 rounded-2xl p-5 md:p-6 card-hover flex flex-col md:flex-row gap-4">
>             <div class="flex-shrink-0 flex flex-col items-center md:items-start">
>               <div class="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-slate-800 flex items-center justify-center mono-accent text-xs text-cyan-300 border border-cyan-500/40">
>                 01
>                     </div>
>               <span class="mt-2 text-[0.7rem] tracking-[0.25em] uppercase text-slate-500 mono-accent">
>                 Start Here
>               </span>

>             <div class="flex-1 space-y-2">
>               <h3 class="text-lg md:text-xl font-semibold text-white">
>                 Foundations &amp; Orientation
>               </h3>
>               <p class="text-sm md:text-base text-slate-300">
>                 Big picture: who Cody is, how their brain and life tend to operate, and how this whole ecosystem of docs, portals, and
>                 guides fits together. If you want the “map of the map,” this is it.
>               </p>
>               <div class="flex flex-wrap gap-2 text-[0.7rem] uppercase tracking-wide">
>                 <span class="px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full bg-slate-800 text-slate-300">Overview</span>
>                 <span class="px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full bg-slate-800 text-slate-300">Context</span>
>                 <span class="px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full bg-slate-800 text-slate-300">How to Use This</span>

### Assistant
> You’re right: you’ve got **two competing “index” concepts** jammed into one file (and one of them is literally a second `<!DOCTYPE html>` appended after the first). That will *absolutely* cause weird behavior, broken styles, and “why is nothing consistent” pain.
> 
> Here’s the clean way to keep the best of both, kill the duplicates, and end with a single coherent system.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## What each “index” is best at
> 
> ### Index A (white, multi-screen wizard)
> Best at:
> - “guided onboarding” vibe
> - progress bar + revisit logic
> - short, gentle story flow
> 
> Weakness:
> - not visually aligned with your main site
> - not scalable for a real docs library
> - feels like a standalone app
> 
> ### Index B (dark Tailwind “7 modules trail”)
> Best at:
> - matches qially.me aesthetic
> - already structured like a doc portal
> - scalable: modules, guides, quick-start paths
> 
> Weakness:
> - no progress tracking
> - no “chapters visited” funnel feel
> 
> ---
> 
> ## The correct merge (best of both)
> 
> ### Keep Index B as the canonical `/manual/` landing page
> Because it matches the brand and scales.
> 
> ### Inject Index A’s “loop/progress” into Index B *as a section*, not as a whole separate page
> Meaning:
> - You keep the 7-module trail layout and nav structure
> - You add a **“Start the Guided Loop”** panel near the top (or under “How this manual works”)
> - The loop marks modules as visited using `localStorage`
> - The loop also supports “Resume” and “Revisit”
> 
> This gives you:
> - cinematic onboarding
> - Microsoft KB-style modular trail
> - unified visual language
> - no competing indexes
> 
> ---
> 
> ## What to delete immediately (dup cleanup)
> 
> 1) **Delete the entire first HTML document** from the combined file OR move it to `/manual/loop.html`
> 2) Keep **one** `<!DOCTYPE html> ... </html>` per file. Period.
> 3) Standardize on **one icon loader**:
>    - Use either `unpkg lucide@latest` OR the Cloudflare lucide version, not both.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## How to implement the merge (practical, minimal edits)
> 
> ### Step 1 — Create two files (clean separation)
> - `/manual/index.html` = your Tailwind 7-module landing (Index B)
> - `/manual/loop.html` = your multi-screen guided experience (Index A) but restyled later
> 
> Then on `/manual/index.html`, add a CTA:
> - “Start the Guided Loop” → `/manual/loop.html`
> 
> This is the fastest “clean” win.
> 
> ### Step 2 — (Better) Pull the loop *into* `/manual/index.html` without the screens
> Instead of “screens,” convert Index A into a **Guided Start widget**:
> 
> - Shows progress bar (0/7)
> - Shows “Continue where you left off”
> - Shows 3 suggested next modules
> - Shows completed list
> 
> This keeps everything static and simple.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## The unified progress model (so everything tracks completion consistently)
> 
> Use one storage key namespace across the entire site:
> 
> - `kb_complete:module-01`
> - `kb_complete:module-02`
> - etc.
> 
> Then your docs pages can also mark completion.
> 
> ### Drop-in progress code (works with your Tailwind page)
> 
> Add this near the bottom of `/manual/index.html` before `</body>`:
> 
> ```html
> <script>
>   const MODULES = [
>     { id: "module-01", title: "Foundations & Orientation", href: "/modules/01-foundations-orientation/" },
>     { id: "module-02", title: "Brain, Health & Energy", href: "/modules/02-brain-health-energy/" },
>     { id: "module-03", title: "Relationships & Boundaries", href: "/modules/03-relationships-boundaries/" },
>     { id: "module-04", title: "Work, Money & Systems", href: "/modules/04-work-money-systems/" },
>     { id: "module-05", title: "Safety, Overwhelm & Crisis", href: "/modules/05-safety-overwhelm-crisis/" },
>     { id: "module-06", title: "Family, History & Context", href: "/modules/06-family-history-context/" },
>     { id: "module-07", title: "Meaning, Values & Purpose", href: "/modules/07-meaning-values-purpose/" },
>   ];
> 
>   function isComplete(id){
>     try { return localStorage.getItem(`kb_complete:${id}`) === "1"; } catch { return false; }
>   }
> 
>   function setComplete(id, val=true){
>     try { localStorage.setItem(`kb_complete:${id}`, val ? "1" : "0"); } catch {}
>   }
> 
>   function computeProgress(){
>     const done = MODULES.filter(m => isComplete(m.id)).length;
>     const total = MODULES.length;
>     const pct = Math.round((done / total) * 100);
>     return { done, total, pct };
>   }
> 
>   function nextModule(){
>     return MODULES.find(m => !isComplete(m.id)) || null;
>   }
> 
>   // Optional: mark visited when they click “Enter the Module”
>   function wireModuleLinks(){
>     document.querySelectorAll("[data-module-id]").forEach(a => {
>       a.addEventListener("click", () => {
>         const id = a.getAttribute("data-module-id");
>         if (id) setComplete(id, true);
>       });
>     });
>   }
> 
>   function renderProgress(){
>     const elText = document.getElementById("manual-progress-text");
>     const elBar  = document.getElementById("manual-progress-bar");
>     const elNext = document.getElementById("manual-next-link");
>     const elList = document.getElementById("manual-completed-list");
> 
>     const { done, total, pct } = computeProgress();
>     if (elText) elText.textContent = `${done}/${total} modules visited (${pct}%)`;
>     if (elBar) elBar.style.width = pct + "%";
> 
>     const next = nextModule();
>     if (elNext){
>       if (next){
>         elNext.href = next.href;
>         elNext.textContent = `Continue: ${next.title}`;
>         elNext.classList.remove("hidden");
>       } else {
>         elNext.classList.add("hidden");
>       }
>     }
> 
>     if (elList){
>       const completed = MODULES.filter(m => isComplete(m.id));
>       elList.innerHTML = completed.length
>         ? completed.map(m => `<a class="inline-flex px-3 py-2 rounded-full bg-slate-800 text-slate-200 text-xs hover:bg-slate-700" href="${m.href}">${m.title}</a>`).join("")
>         : `<span class="text-slate-500 text-sm">No modules completed yet.</span>`;
>     }
>   }
> 
>   wireModuleLinks();
>   renderProgress();
> </script>
> ```
> 
> ### Then add this “Guided Loop” UI block to your Tailwind page
> Put it right under your hero or under “How This Manual Works”:
> 
> ```html
> <section class="bg-slate-900 rounded-2xl p-6 md:p-8 border border-slate-800">
>   <div class="flex items-start justify-between gap-6 flex-wrap">
>     <div>
>       <h2 class="text-2xl md:text-3xl font-bold text-white mb-2">Guided Loop</h2>
>       <p class="text-slate-400 text-sm md:text-base max-w-2xl">
>         This tracks what you’ve already covered. You can continue where you left off, or revisit completed modules.
>       </p>
>     </div>
>     <a id="manual-next-link" href="#" class="hidden inline-flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2 rounded-full bg-cyan-500 text-slate-950 text-sm font-semibold hover:bg-cyan-400 transition-colors">
>       Continue
>       <i data-lucide="arrow-right" class="w-4 h-4"></i>
>     </a>
>   </div>
> 
>   <div class="mt-5">
>     <p id="manual-progress-text" class="text-xs text-slate-400 mb-2">0/7 modules visited (0%)</p>
>     <div class="h-2 rounded-full bg-slate-800 overflow-hidden">
>       <div id="manual-progress-bar" class="h-2 bg-cyan-500" style="width:0%"></div>
>     </div>
>   </div>
> 
>   <div class="mt-5">
>     <p class="text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.25em] text-slate-500 mb-2">Completed</p>
>     <div id="manual-completed-list" class="flex flex-wrap gap-2"></div>
>   </div>
> </section>
> ```
> 
> ### Finally: tag your module links so clicks mark completion
> Change each “Enter the Module” link like:
> 
> ```html
> <a data-module-id="module-01" href="/modules/01-foundations-orientation/" ...>Enter the Module</a>
> ```
> 
> Do that for module 01–07.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## What you end up with (the best of both)
> - One canonical `/manual/` landing page (dark, coherent, scalable)
> - A guided loop/progress system (from the wizard)
> - No duplicate indexes
> - Everything still “static site friendly”
> 
> ---
> 
> ## My blunt call
> Don’t try to keep the full multi-screen wizard AND the 7-module trail on the same page right now. You’ll bloat and confuse the user.
> 
> Do **this**:
> - `/manual/index.html` = Tailwind trail + progress widget
> - `/manual/loop.html` = optional full “story mode” later
> 
> If you want, paste your current `/manual/index.html` (the Tailwind one) and tell me your desired final URLs (`/modules/...` vs `/docs/...`). I’ll return a fully merged single-file HTML with:
> - the Guided Loop block inserted
> - `data-module-id` wired everywhere
> - consistent lucide import
> - no duplicate head/body garbage.

### User
> ok can you give the the updated html for both the index and loop, I like the idea you suggesting.

### Assistant
> Below are **two clean, production-ready static files**:
> 
> - `/manual/index.html` → your **canonical Manual landing** (Tailwind “7 modules trail”) **plus** the Guided Loop progress widget.
> - `/manual/loop.html` → your **guided multi-screen loop** (the “Begin the Story” flow) restyled to match your dark/glass aesthetic, and wired to the **same completion keys** (`kb_complete:module-0X`).
> 
> They share one progress model, so completion stays consistent no matter how the user navigates.
>

>     <p class="mb-1">Built as a living manual. Thanks for caring enough to read it.</p>

>     </p>
>   </footer>
> 
>   <script>
>     // Icons
>     if (window.lucide) lucide.createIcons();
> 
>     // Progress model: kb_complete:module-0X
>     const MODULES = [
>       { id: "module-01", title: "Foundations & Orientation", href: "/modules/01-foundations-orientation/" },
>       { id: "module-02", title: "Brain, Health & Energy", href: "/modules/02-brain-health-energy/" },
>       { id: "module-03", title: "Relationships & Boundaries", href: "/modules/03-relationships-boundaries/" },
>       { id: "module-04", title: "Work, Money & Systems", href: "/modules/04-work-money-systems/" },
>       { id: "module-05", title: "Safety, Overwhelm & Crisis", href: "/modules/05-safety-overwhelm-crisis/" },
>       { id: "module-06", title: "Family, History & Context", href: "/modules/06-family-history-context/" },
>       { id: "module-07", title: "Meaning, Values & Purpose", href: "/modules/07-meaning-values-purpose/" },
>     ];
> 
>     function isComplete(id){
>       try { return localStorage.getItem(`kb_complete:${id}`) === "1"; } catch { return false; }
>     }
>     function setComplete(id, val=true){
>       try { localStorage.setItem(`kb_complete:${id}`, val ? "1" : "0"); } catch {}
>     }
>     function computeProgress(){
>       const done = MODULES.filter(m => isComplete(m.id)).length;
>       const total = MODULES.length;
>       const pct = Math.round((done / total) * 100);
>       return { done, total, pct };
>     }
>     function nextModule(){
>       return MODULES.find(m => !isComplete(m.id)) || null;
>     }
> 
>     // Mark completion on click for module links
>     function wireModuleLinks(){
>       document.querySelectorAll("[data-module-id]").forEach(a => {
>         a.addEventListener("click", () => {
>           const id = a.getAttribute("data-module-id");
>           if (id) setComplete(id, true);
>         });
>       });
>     }
> 
>     function resetProgress(){
>       MODULES.forEach(m => setComplete(m.id, false));
>       renderProgress();
>     }
> 
>     function renderProgress(){
>       const elText = document.getElementById("manual-progress-text");
>       const elBar  = document.getElementById("manual-progress-bar");
>       const elNext = document.getElementById("manual-next-link");
>       const elList = document.getElementById("manual-completed-list");
> 
>       const { done, total, pct } = computeProgress();
> 
>       if (elText) elText.textContent = `${done}/${total} modules visited (${pct}%)`;
>       if (elBar)  elBar.style.width = pct + "%";
> 
>       const next = nextModule();
>       if (elNext){
>         if (next){
>           elNext.href = next.href;
>           elNext.textContent = `Continue: ${next.title}`;
>           elNext.classList.remove("hidden");
>         } else {
>           elNext.classList.add("hidden");
>         }
>       }
> 
>       if (elList){
>         const completed = MODULES.filter(m => isComplete(m.id));
>         elList.innerHTML = completed.length
>           ? completed.map(m => `<a class="inline-flex px-3 py-2 rounded-full bg-slate-800 text-slate-200 text-xs hover:bg-slate-700" href="${m.href}">${m.title}</a>`).join("")
>           : `<span class="text-slate-500 text-sm">No modules completed yet.</span>`;
>       }
> 
>       // Icons inside injected HTML (completed list doesn’t include icons but safe)
>       if (window.lucide) lucide.createIcons();
>     }
> 
>     document.getElementById("manual-reset")?.addEventListener("click", resetProgress);
> 
>     wireModuleLinks();
>     renderProgress();
>   </script>
> </body>
> </html>
> ```
> 
> ---
> 
> # 2) `/manual/loop.html` (guided “story mode” that syncs progress)
> 
> This uses the same module IDs and marks completion when screens are visited.
