>             Revisit Chapters
>           </button>
>           <a class="px-5 py-3 rounded-full border border-white/10 text-slate-200 hover:bg-slate-800 transition"
>              href="/manual/#trail">
>             Go to Modules
>           </a>
>         </div>
>       </div>
>     </section>
> 
>   </main>
> 
>   <script>
>     if (window.lucide) lucide.createIcons();
> 
>     // Loop Chapters map to MODULE completion keys
>     const CHAPTERS = [
>       { id: 'learn', title: 'Learn / How My World Works', screen: 'screen-learn', moduleId: 'module-01' },
>       { id: 'health', title: 'Health / Brain & Body', screen: 'screen-health', moduleId: 'module-02' },
>       { id: 'relationships', title: 'Relationships / Boundaries', screen: 'screen-relationships', moduleId: 'module-03' }
>     ];
> 
>     const LOOP_KEY = 'manual_loop_progress_v1';
> 
>     function kbSetComplete(moduleId, val=true){
>       try { localStorage.setItem(`kb_complete:${moduleId}`, val ? "1" : "0"); } catch {}
>     }
> 
>     function getVisited(){
>       try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(LOOP_KEY)) || []; } catch { return []; }
>     }
>     function setVisited(v){
>       try { localStorage.setItem(LOOP_KEY, JSON.stringify(v)); } catch {}
>     }
> 
>     function markVisited(chapterId){
>       const visited = getVisited();
>       if (!visited.includes(chapterId)){
>         visited.push(chapterId);
>         setVisited(visited);
>       }
>       const chapter = CHAPTERS.find(c => c.id === chapterId);
>       if (chapter?.moduleId) kbSetComplete(chapter.moduleId, true);
> 
>       updateProgressUI();
>     }
> 
>     function showScreen(id){
>       document.querySelectorAll('.screen').forEach(s => s.classList.remove('active'));
>       const target = document.getElementById(id);
>       if (target){
>         target.classList.add('active');
>         window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
>       }
>       const chapter = CHAPTERS.find(c => c.screen === id);
>       if (chapter) markVisited(chapter.id);
> 
>       if (window.lucide) lucide.createIcons();
>     }
> 
>     function updateProgressUI(){
>       const visited = getVisited();
> 
>       const progressText = document.getElementById('progress-text');
>       const progressBar = document.getElementById('progress-bar');
>       const completedList = document.getElementById('completed-list');
>       const choiceButtons = document.getElementById('choice-buttons');
> 
>       const total = CHAPTERS.length;
>       const done = visited.length;
>       const percent = Math.round((done / total) * 100);
> 
>       if (progressText) progressText.textContent = `${done}/${total} chapters visited (${percent}%)`;
>       if (progressBar) progressBar.style.width = percent + '%';
> 
>       const remaining = CHAPTERS.filter(c => !visited.includes(c.id));
>       const completed = CHAPTERS.filter(c => visited.includes(c.id));
> 
>       if (choiceButtons){
>         choiceButtons.innerHTML = '';
>         if (remaining.length === 0){
>           const doneBtn = document.createElement('button');
>           doneBtn.className = 'w-full px-5 py-3 rounded-full bg-cyan-500 text-slate-950 font-semibold hover:bg-cyan-400 transition';
>           doneBtn.textContent = 'Finish this loop';
>           doneBtn.onclick = () => showScreen('screen-complete');
>           choiceButtons.appendChild(doneBtn);
>         } else {
>           remaining.forEach(ch => {
>             const btn = document.createElement('button');
>             btn.className = 'w-full px-5 py-3 rounded-full bg-cyan-500 text-slate-950 font-semibold hover:bg-cyan-400 transition text-left';
>             btn.textContent = ch.title;
>             btn.onclick = () => showScreen(ch.screen);
>             choiceButtons.appendChild(btn);
>           });
>         }
>       }
> 
>       if (completedList){
>         completedList.innerHTML = '';
>         if (completed.length > 0){
>           const header = document.createElement('p');
>           header.className = 'text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.25em] text-slate-500 mb-3';
>           header.textContent = 'Revisit a completed chapter:';
>           completedList.appendChild(header);
> 
>           const wrap = document.createElement('div');
>           wrap.className = 'flex flex-col gap-2';
> 
>           completed.forEach(ch => {
>             const btn = document.createElement('button');
>             btn.className = 'px-4 py-2 rounded-full border border-white/10 text-slate-200 hover:bg-slate-800 transition text-left';
>             btn.textContent = ch.title;
>             btn.onclick = () => showScreen(ch.screen);
>             wrap.appendChild(btn);
>           });
> 
>           completedList.appendChild(wrap);
>         }
>       }
>     }
> 
>     // Wire generic button nav
>     document.querySelectorAll('button[data-go]').forEach(btn => {
>       btn.addEventListener('click', () => showScreen(btn.getAttribute('data-go')));
>     });
> 
>     // Mark completion if they click module links inside screens
>     document.querySelectorAll('[data-module-id]').forEach(a => {
>       a.addEventListener('click', () => {
>         const id = a.getAttribute('data-module-id');
>         if (id) kbSetComplete(id, true);
>       });
>     });
> 
>     // Reset loop (only loop, not whole manual)
>     document.getElementById('loop-reset')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
>       try { localStorage.removeItem(LOOP_KEY); } catch {}
>       updateProgressUI();
>     });
> 
>     updateProgressUI();
>   </script>
> </body>
> </html>
> ```
> 
> ---
> 
> ## What you need to change (only placeholders)
> - Replace `VIDEO_ID_OVERVIEW`, `VIDEO_ID_LEARN`, `VIDEO_ID_HEALTH`, `VIDEO_ID_RELATIONSHIPS`
> - Replace `PLAYLIST_ID_INTRO`
> - Update module URLs if your real paths are `/docs/modules/...` instead of `/modules/...`
> 
> ---
> 
> ## File placement
> - `public/manual/index.html`
> - `public/manual/loop.html`
> (Or your repo equivalent.)
> 
> If you paste your actual desired module folder structure (exact URLs you want), I’ll adjust both files so every link matches your final routing with zero guesswork.

> Minimal static site builder that pulls assets and HTML docs from QiVault.
> 
> Quick Start
> Edit site_config.json to specify which files from QiVault to include
> Run the build: python build.py
> Deploy: Push root directory to Cloudflare Pages (index.html at root)
> Structure
> qially-me-v2.0/
> ├── build.py              # Build script
> ├── site_config.json      # Configuration (which files to include)
> ├── templates/
> │   └── index_base.html   # HTML template
> ├── index.html            # Built output (at root)
> ├── images/               # Images (at root)
> ├── docs/                 # HTML documents (at root)
> ├── sections/             # Section pages for URL access control (at root)
> ├── assets/               # Assets (at root)
> └── README.md
> Configuration
> Edit site_config.json to add:
> 
> Assets: Images, small videos, etc. (must be < 25 MiB for Cloudflare Pages)
> HTML Docs: HTML files from QiVault to include
> Featured Video: YouTube or Cloudflare Stream embed
> Example Config
> {
>   "assets": [
>     {
>       "vault_path": "02_clinical/.../assets/image.png",
>       "public_path": "assets/image.png"
>     }
>   ],
>   "html_docs": [
>     {
>       "vault_path": "02_clinical/.../html/doc.html",
>       "slug": "doc_slug",
>       "title": "Document Title"
>     }
>   ],
>   "featured_video": {
>     "type": "youtube",
>     "id": "VIDEO_ID_HERE"
>   }
> }
> Video Handling
> Small Videos (< 25 MiB)
> Add to assets in config
> Will be copied directly to site
> Large Videos
> YouTube: Upload as unlisted, add ID to featured_video config
> Cloudflare Stream: Upload to Stream, add video ID to config
> R2: Store in R2 bucket, link directly in HTML
> Deployment
> Build: python build.py (creates index.html and folders at root)
> Commit and push root directory
> Point Cloudflare Pages to root directory (Output Directory: / or empty)
> Auto-deploys on push
> Paths
> Vault Root: C:\QiOS_v1\realms\qivault\kb\1_Life (edit in build.py if different)
> Output: Root directory (index.html, images/, docs/, sections/, assets/)
> Cloudflare: Set Output Directory to / or empty (serves from root)

### Assistant
> Got it. This README is the “truth” of what we’re building, and it explains why you ended up with competing indexes.
> 
> ## What we’re actually building (so you stop drifting)
> **Cody Home Center** is a **minimal static site builder** that:
> 
> 1. **Pulls pre-written HTML + assets from QiVault**
> 2. **Copies them into a Cloudflare Pages-friendly root output**
> 3. **Generates a root `index.html` (from `templates/index_base.html`)**
> 4. Deploy is just: `python build.py` → push repo → Pages serves from root
> 
> So: **this is not a React app** and not a full SPA. It’s a **compiled static site** with simple routes like:
> - `/index.html`
> - `/docs/<slug>.html` (or whatever the builder emits)
> - `/sections/<something>.html` (for “access control” entry points)
> - `/assets/*`
> 
> That means we need **one canonical landing** and the “Manual to Me” UI should be **one or more HTML docs** that get copied into `/docs/` (or `/manual/`) and then linked from the main index.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## Why you had “competing indexs”
> You had:
> - A standalone, self-contained **manual loop HTML** (multi-screen JS app)
> - A more polished **Tailwind landing page** with “modules trail”
> 
> Both were valid — but your builder architecture expects **ONE root index**. Everything else should be docs/sections.
> 
> So the merge strategy is:
> 
> ### Keep
> - The Tailwind “trail / 7 modules” design as the **main Manual page**
> - The guided “loop” as a **separate page** (not the root index)
> 
> ### Remove / Avoid
> - Multiple full HTML documents jammed into one file
> - Multiple different progress systems
> 
> ### Unify
> - One progress model in localStorage:
>   - `kb_complete:module-01` … `kb_complete:module-07`
>   - Loop chapters mark module completion for 01–03
> 
> ---
> 
> ## How this maps to your builder output
> Your repo structure says:
> - Root output must contain `index.html`
> - Docs should live in `/docs/`
> - “Section pages” live in `/sections/`
> 
> So the cleanest build target is:
> 
> - **Root**: `index.html` = Cody Home Center landing (not the manual itself)
> - **Docs**:
>   - `/docs/manual.html` = the Manual landing (7 modules + progress)
>   - `/docs/manual-loop.html` = the guided loop
> 
> And your root `index.html` links into those.
> 
> If you *want* the Manual to be the home page, you still keep the builder — you just make the generated `index.html` essentially a wrapper that immediately presents the manual.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## What I need from you (fast, no drama)
> Before I rewrite your actual `templates/index_base.html` to generate the final output, answer this by choosing one:
> 
> ### Option A (recommended)
> **Root index = Cody Home Center**, with buttons:
> - Manual to Me
> - Updates
> - Donation / status / etc.
> …and Manual lives in `/docs/manual.html`
> 
> ### Option B
> **Root index = Manual to Me**, and “Home Center” stuff becomes links inside the manual.
> 
> Pick A or B.
> 
> ---
>

### Assistant
> Yes. And you’re right to ditch builds if the goal is “update from my phone in the GitHub app.” Builds are friction, and friction kills consistency.
> 
> Here’s the clean mental model:
> 
> - **Landing page** = “What is this + choose your path”
> - **Quick Facts** = short articles with optional deep-dive sections (audio/video/docs) and cross-links
> - **Guided Path** = the “loop” onboarding experience (learning module vibe + completion tracking)
> - **Manual (10 pages)** = a specific artifact (HTML page or PDF) linked as “Manual v1”
> 
> ### Guided loop vs learning modules
> They’re not different in outcome. The difference is format:
> - **Guided loop** = curated onboarding flow (best for family).
> - **Learning modules** = same content but navigable like docs (best for “let me browse” people).
> 
> So we merge the *concept*: **the Guided Path is the Learning Modules experience**, just presented as a “story loop.”
>

>

>       {

>         title: "Step 1 — Foundations",

>           </div>
>         `
>       },
>       {
>         id: "brain-body",
>         title: "Step 2 — Brain & Body",
>         kicker: "ADHD + nervous system",
>         badge: "02",
>         icon: "activity",
>         summary: "What overwhelm looks like, what shutdown looks like, and how to support without escalating.",
>         deepLinks: [
>           { label: "Related fact: ADHD & overload", href: "/facts/adhd/" },
>           { label: "Media hub", href: "/media/" }
>         ],
>         content: `
>           <h2 class="text-2xl md:text-3xl font-bold text-slate-100">Brain & Body</h2>
>           <p class="mt-3 text-slate-400">
>             On hard days, it can look like avoidance or distance. Often it’s not. It’s regulation.
>           </p>
> 
>           <div class="mt-6 rounded-xl bg-slate-950/50 border border-white/5 p-4">
>             <div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-slate-200 font-semibold">
>               <i data-lucide="alert-triangle" class="w-4 h-4 text-amber-300"></i>
>               The rule
>             </div>
>             <p class="mt-2 text-sm text-slate-300">

>               One ask. One channel. One time window.

>         id: "relationships",
>         title: "Step 3 — Relationships & Boundaries",
>         kicker: "How to avoid misfires",
>         badge: "03",
>         icon: "shield",
>         summary: "Boundaries, repair, and how to address conflict without triggering shutdown or escalation.",
>         deepLinks: [
>           { label: "Related fact: Boundaries", href: "/facts/boundaries/" },
>           { label: "Manual v1", href: "/manual/" }
>         ],
>         content: `
>           <h2 class="text-2xl md:text-3xl font-bold text-slate-100">Relationships & Boundaries</h2>
>           <p class="mt-3 text-slate-400">
>             Cody is direct. That’s not a character flaw. It’s a compression strategy.
>           </p>
> 
>           <div class="mt-6 rounded-xl bg-slate-950/50 border border-white/5 p-4">
>             <div class="text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-slate-500 mb-2">Conflict protocol</div>
>             <ol class="space-y-2 text-sm text-slate-300 list-decimal list-inside">
>               <li><span class="font-semibold">Pause.</span> Name the goal (repair, not punishment).</li>
>               <li>State one issue, one example, one ask.</li>
>               <li>Give a time window to respond.</li>
>             </ol>
>           </div>
> 
>           <div class="mt-6 grid md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
>             <div class="rounded-xl bg-slate-950/50 border border-white/5 p-4">
>               <div class="text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-slate-500 mb-2">Soft boundary</div>
>               <p class="text-sm text-slate-300 italic">“I can’t do that right now, but I can do X.”</p>
>             </div>
>             <div class="rounded-xl bg-slate-950/50 border border-white/5 p-4">
>               <div class="text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-slate-500 mb-2">Hard boundary</div>
>               <p class="text-sm text-slate-300 italic">“No. That doesn’t align with my priorities.”</p>
>             </div>
>           </div>
>         `
>       }
>     ];
> 
>     function getState() {
>       try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY)) || { done: [] }; }
>       catch { return { done: [] }; }
>     }
> 
>     function setState(state) {
>       localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(state));
>     }
> 
>     function markDone(id) {
>       const state = getState();
>       if (!state.done.includes(id)) state.done.push(id);
>       setState(state);
>       renderProgress();
>     }
> 
>     function resetProgress() {
>       localStorage.removeItem(STORAGE_KEY);
>       renderProgress();
>       renderScreen("home");
>     }
> 
>     function renderProgress() {
>       const state = getState();
>       const done = state.done.length;
>       const total = STEPS.length;
>       const pct = Math.round((done / total) * 100);
> 
>       document.getElementById("progressText").textContent = `${done}/${total} completed`;
>       document.getElementById("progressPct").textContent = `${pct}%`;
>       document.getElementById("progressBar").style.width = `${pct}%`;
>     }
> 
>     function stepCard(step) {
>       const state = getState();
>       const completed = state.done.includes(step.id);
> 
>       const links = (step.deepLinks || [])
>         .map(l => `<a class="text-sm text-slate-300 hover:text-emerald-300 underline underline-offset-4" href="${l.href}">${l.label}</a>`)
>         .join(`<span class="text-slate-600"> · </span>`);
> 
>       return `
>         <div class="rounded-2xl border border-white/5 bg-slate-950/40 p-5 hover:bg-slate-950/55 transition">
>           <div class="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
>             <div class="flex items-center gap-3">
>               <div class="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl bg-white/5 border border-white/10 flex items-center justify-center">
>                 <i data-lucide="${step.icon}" class="w-5 h-5 text-slate-200"></i>
>               </div>
>               <div>
>                 <div class="text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-slate-500">${step.kicker}</div>
>                 <div class="text-lg font-semibold text-slate-100">${step.title}</div>
>               </div>
>             </div>
> 
>             <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
>               ${completed ? `<span class="text-xs font-semibold text-emerald-300 bg-emerald-500/10 border border-emerald-500/20 px-2 py-1 rounded-full">Done</span>` : ``}
>               <span class="text-xs font-semibold text-slate-300 bg-white/5 border border-white/10 px-2 py-1 rounded-full">${step.badge}</span>
>             </div>
>           </div>
> 
>           <p class="mt-3 text-sm text-slate-400">${step.summary}</p>
> 
>           <div class="mt-4 flex flex-wrap items-center gap-3">
>             <button class="inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-sm font-semibold bg-emerald-500/15 border border-emerald-500/20 hover:bg-emerald-500/20"
>               onclick="openStep('${step.id}')">
>               Start
>               <i data-lucide="arrow-right" class="w-4 h-4"></i>
>             </button>
> 
>             <div class="text-xs text-slate-500">
>               ${links || ""}
>             </div>
>           </div>
>         </div>
>       `;
>     }
> 
>     function renderScreen(mode, stepId) {
>       const screen = document.getElementById("screen");
> 
>       if (mode === "home") {
>         screen.innerHTML = `
>           <div class="animate-fadeIn">
>             <div class="flex items-center justify-between gap-4 flex-wrap">
>               <div>
>                 <div class="text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-slate-500">Choose a step</div>
>                 <h2 class="mt-2 text-2xl md:text-3xl font-bold text-slate-100">Where do you want to start?</h2>
>                 <p class="mt-2 text-sm md:text-base text-slate-400 max-w-2xl">
>                   If you’re worried about Cody right now, start with <span class="text-slate-200 font-semibold">Brain & Body</span>.
>                   If you’re confused about relationship tension, start with <span class="text-slate-200 font-semibold">Relationships & Boundaries</span>.
>                 </p>
>               </div>
> 
>               <a href="/facts/" class="inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-sm font-semibold bg-white/5 border border-white/10 hover:bg-white/10">
>                 <i data-lucide="file-text" class="w-4 h-4"></i>
>                 Or browse facts
>               </a>
>             </div>
> 
>             <div class="mt-6 grid gap-4">
>               ${STEPS.map(stepCard).join("")}
>             </div>
>           </div>
>         `;
>         lucide.createIcons();
>         return;
>       }
> 
>       const step = STEPS.find(s => s.id === stepId);
>       if (!step) return renderScreen("home");
> 
>       screen.innerHTML = `
>         <div class="animate-fadeIn">
>           <div class="flex items-center justify-between gap-3 flex-wrap">
>             <button class="inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-sm font-semibold bg-white/5 border border-white/10 hover:bg-white/10"
>               onclick="renderScreen('home')">
>               <i data-lucide="chevron-left" class="w-4 h-4"></i>
>               Back
>             </button>
> 
>             <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
>               <span class="text-xs font-semibold text-slate-300 bg-white/5 border border-white/10 px-2 py-1 rounded-full">${step.badge}</span>
>             </div>
>           </div>
> 
>           <div class="mt-5">
>             ${step.content}
>           </div>
> 
>           <div class="mt-7 flex flex-wrap gap-3">
>             <button class="inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-sm font-semibold bg-emerald-500/15 border border-emerald-500/20 hover:bg-emerald-500/20"
>               onclick="completeStep('${step.id}')">
>               Mark complete
>               <i data-lucide="check-circle" class="w-4 h-4"></i>
>             </button>
> 
>             <button class="inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-sm font-semibold bg-white/5 border border-white/10 hover:bg-white/10"
>               onclick="goNext('${step.id}')">
>               Next
>               <i data-lucide="arrow-right" class="w-4 h-4"></i>
>             </button>
>           </div>
> 
>           ${(step.deepLinks && step.deepLinks.length)
>             ? `<div class="mt-6 text-sm text-slate-400">
>                  <div class="text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-slate-500 mb-2">Optional deep dives</div>
>                  <div class="flex flex-col gap-2">
>                    ${step.deepLinks.map(l => `<a class="text-slate-300 hover:text-emerald-300 underline underline-offset-4" href="${l.href}">${l.label}</a>`).join("")}
>                  </div>
>                </div>`
>             : ``}
>         </div>
>       `;
>       lucide.createIcons();
>     }
> 
>     // Expose functions to onclick
>     window.openStep = (id) => renderScreen("step", id);
> 
>     window.completeStep = (id) => {
>       markDone(id);
>       // stay on page, just updates progress
>     };
> 
>     window.goNext = (id) => {
>       const idx = STEPS.findIndex(s => s.id === id);
>       if (idx === -1) return renderScreen("home");
>       const next = STEPS[idx + 1];
>       if (next) renderScreen("step", next.id);
>       else renderScreen("home");
>     };
> 
>     document.getElementById("resetBtn").addEventListener("click", resetProgress);
> 
>     // init
>     renderProgress();
>     renderScreen("home");
>   </script>
> </body>
> </html>
> ```

> 
> ## What’s missing (and what you should paste next)
> To finish this properly (and fast), paste **one** of your existing “Facts article pages” (any one), and I’ll give you a reusable **Facts Article Template** that includes:
> 
> - “Quick answer” section at top
> - “Deep dive” anchor jump
> - optional audio embed + YouTube embed blocks
> - “Related facts” cards (cross-linking)
> - a “Mark read” progress toggle (same localStorage pattern)
> 
> That’s the last piece that turns this from “pretty pages” into a coherent personal docs system.

### User
> look at my ugle site i got stuff everywhere. this is good content just need everything organized.

### Assistant
> You’re right: you had **competing “index” concepts** fighting each other.
> 
> - **Index A (Docs Sidebar App)** = great *knowledge base navigation* (lots of pages, expandable sections).
> - **Index B (Manual Loop / Story Screens)** = great *onboarding + completion progress* (guided path, “finish this loop”).
> 
> Best-of-both move:
> - Keep **Index A** as the **site’s main landing / router** (simple choices + links).
> - Keep **Index B** as a **dedicated guided experience** at `/loop/` (progress + chapters + playlists).
> - Everything else becomes **static folder pages** (`/facts/.../index.html`, `/modules/.../index.html`, `/manual/.../index.html`) so your directory mirrors your nav.
> 
> Below are **two ready-to-drop static files**: **root `index.html`** + **`/loop/index.html`**. They share styling and use **localStorage** for completion/progress. No build step. GitHub app friendly.
> 
> ---
> 
> ```html
> <!-- FILE: index.html -->
> <!doctype html>

>   <script>
>     const YEAR = document.getElementById('y');
>     YEAR.textContent = new Date().getFullYear();
> 
>     // Guided Loop progress mini-widget
>     // Shared with /loop/ by using the same storage key + chapter count.
>     const STORAGE_KEY = 'cody_home_loop_v1';
>     const LOOP_TOTAL = 7;
> 
>     function getLoopState(){
>       try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY)) || { visited: [] }; }
>       catch { return { visited: [] }; }
>     }
> 
>     const st = getLoopState();
>     const done = Array.isArray(st.visited) ? st.visited.length : 0;
>     const pct = Math.round((Math.min(done, LOOP_TOTAL) / LOOP_TOTAL) * 100);
> 
>     document.getElementById('progress-mini').textContent = `${pct}%`;
>     document.getElementById('bar-mini').style.width = `${pct}%`;
> 
>     if (window.lucide) lucide.createIcons();
>   </script>
> </body>
> </html>
> ```

>             Quick Facts

>           </a>
>           <a href="/manual/" class="px-5 py-3 rounded-full border border-white/10 hover:border-white/20 hover:bg-white/5 transition inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
>             Full Manual
>             <i data-lucide="book-open" class="w-4 h-4"></i>
>           </a>

>       </div>
>     </section>
> 
>     <footer class="pt-8 border-t border-white/5 text-xs text-slate-500 flex flex-col md:flex-row justify-between gap-3">
>       <div>© <span id="y"></span> Cody • Guided Loop</div>
>       <div class="mono">/loop/</div>
>     </footer>
>   </main>
> 
>   <script>
>     const STORAGE_KEY = 'cody_home_loop_v1';
> 
>     const MODULES = [
>       {
>         id: 'm1',
>         n: 1,

>             <li>Assume good intent; optimize for written context.</li>
>           </ul>
>         `,
>         deep: 'Deep dive: the “why” behind documentation, async communication, and how to interpret tone.',

>         `,

>             <li>Support means alignment, not control.</li>

>         videoId: 'VIDEO_ID'
>       }
>     ];
> 
>     function getState(){
>       try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY)) || { visited: [] }; }
>       catch { return { visited: [] }; }
>     }
>     function setState(st){ localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(st)); }
> 
>     function markVisited(moduleId){
>       const st = getState();
>       if (!Array.isArray(st.visited)) st.visited = [];
>       if (!st.visited.includes(moduleId)) st.visited.push(moduleId);
>       setState(st);
>       updateProgress();
>     }
> 
>     function updateProgress(){
>       const st = getState();
>       const done = Array.isArray(st.visited) ? st.visited.length : 0;
>       const total = MODULES.length;
>       const pct = Math.round((Math.min(done, total) / total) * 100);
> 
>       document.getElementById('progressText').textContent = `${done}/${total}`;
>       document.getElementById('progressPct').textContent = `${pct}%`;
>       document.getElementById('progressBar').style.width = `${pct}%`;
> 
>       // Hub: build module grid
>       const grid = document.getElementById('moduleGrid');
>       const revisitBox = document.getElementById('revisitBox');
>       const revisitList = document.getElementById('revisitList');
> 
>       if (grid){
>         grid.innerHTML = '';
>         MODULES.forEach(m => {
>           const visited = Array.isArray(st.visited) && st.visited.includes(m.id);
>           const pill = visited
>             ? `<span class="text-[11px] px-2 py-1 rounded-full bg-emerald-500/15 border border-emerald-500/20 text-emerald-200 mono">Visited</span>`
>             : `<span class="text-[11px] px-2 py-1 rounded-full bg-white/5 border border-white/10 text-slate-300 mono">Not yet</span>`;
> 
>           const el = document.createElement('button');
>           el.className = 'text-left rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-5 hover:bg-white/[0.07] hover:border-white/20 transition';
>           el.innerHTML = `
>             <div class="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
>               <div>
>                 <div class="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.22em] text-slate-500 mono">Module ${m.n}</div>
>                 <div class="mt-1 font-semibold text-white">${m.title}</div>
>                 <div class="mt-2 text-sm text-slate-400">${m.desc}</div>
>               </div>
>               <div class="shrink-0">${pill}</div>
>             </div>
>           `;
>           el.onclick = () => openModule(m.id);
>           grid.appendChild(el);
>         });
>       }
> 
>       // Revisit list
>       const completed = MODULES.filter(m => Array.isArray(st.visited) && st.visited.includes(m.id));
>       if (revisitBox && revisitList){
>         if (completed.length > 0){
>           revisitBox.classList.remove('hidden');
>           revisitList.innerHTML = '';
>           completed.forEach(m => {
>             const b = document.createElement('button');
>             b.className = 'text-xs px-3 py-2 rounded-full border border-white/10 hover:border-white/20 hover:bg-white/5 transition';
>             b.textContent = `M${m.n}`;
>             b.onclick = () => openModule(m.id);
>             revisitList.appendChild(b);
>           });
>         } else {
>           revisitBox.classList.add('hidden');
>         }
>       }
> 
>       // Complete screen trigger
>       if (done >= total){
>         // don’t auto-kick them; only show completion if they choose it
>       }
>     }
> 
>     function showScreen(id){
>       document.querySelectorAll('.screen').forEach(s => s.classList.remove('active'));
>       const target = document.getElementById(id);
>       if (target) target.classList.add('active');
>       window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
>       if (window.lucide) lucide.createIcons();
>     }
> 
>     function openModule(moduleId){
>       const m = MODULES.find(x => x.id === moduleId);
>       if (!m) return;
> 
>       document.getElementById('moduleKicker').textContent = `Module ${m.n} of ${MODULES.length}`;
>       document.getElementById('moduleTitle').textContent = m.title;
>       document.getElementById('moduleDesc').textContent = m.desc;
>       document.getElementById('moduleQuick').innerHTML = m.quick;
>       document.getElementById('moduleDeep').textContent = m.deep;
> 
>       const factsLink = document.getElementById('factsLink');
>       const pageLink = document.getElementById('pageLink');
>       factsLink.href = m.factsHref;
>       pageLink.href = m.pageHref;
> 
>       const vf = document.getElementById('videoFrame');
>       vf.src = `https://www.youtube.com/embed/${m.videoId}`;
> 
>       // Mark visited when opened
>       markVisited(m.id);
> 
>       // Next recommended
>       const st = getState();
>       const next = MODULES.find(x => !st.visited.includes(x.id));
>       const nextBtn = document.getElementById('nextBtn');
>       nextBtn.onclick = () => {
>         const st2 = getState();
>         const nxt = MODULES.find(x => !st2.visited.includes(x.id));
>         if (nxt) openModule(nxt.id);
>         else showScreen('screen-complete');
>       };
>       nextBtn.textContent = next ? 'Next recommended module' : 'Finish the loop';
> 
>       showScreen('screen-module');
>     }
> 
>     // Wire generic nav buttons
>     document.querySelectorAll('[data-go]').forEach(btn => {
>       btn.addEventListener('click', () => showScreen(btn.getAttribute('data-go')));
>     });
> 
>     // Reset
>     document.getElementById('resetBtn').addEventListener('click', () => {
>       localStorage.removeItem(STORAGE_KEY);
>       updateProgress();
>       showScreen('screen-hub');
>     });
> 
>     // Footer year
>     document.getElementById('y').textContent = new Date().getFullYear();
> 
>     // Init
>     updateProgress();
>     if (window.lucide) lucide.createIcons();
>   </script>
> </body>
> </html>
> ```
> 
> ---
> 
> If you want the directory to mirror navigation (and stop the “stuff everywhere” problem), use this **static-only folder layout**:
> 
> - `/index.html` (home router)
> - `/loop/index.html` (guided loop)
> - `/facts/<topic>/index.html` (short FAQ + deep dive per topic)
> - `/modules/01-.../index.html` etc (full structured modules)
> - `/manual/index.html` (your “10-page manual” as one page or split pages)
> - `/videos/index.html` (playlists/podcast embeds)
> - `/tools/<tool>/index.html` (questionnaires, self-assessments)
> 
> If you want, paste your current top-level repo tree (just folder/file names), and I’ll give you a ruthless re-org map that preserves content but puts it where it belongs.
